[维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告（2022年11月30日）第86期（共 1459人） （七）](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/2022113086-1459_40.html)
------

<div>

lang="EN-US">X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>）</b><p></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">X.</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">希尔扎提•巴吾东（维吾尔）、<span Roman&quot;;">肖传雄、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐德武</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: 11.0pt;">徐福明、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐光</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 0pt;">徐桂莲</span>、<span style="mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐桂珍、</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐衍贞</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐强、徐秦、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐瑞萍、徐润叶、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐孝兰、徐秀娟、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐永清</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐中惠、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许朝晖、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">许峰</span>、许凤梅、许高瑞、许继梅</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许来福、许丽、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许丽华</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">许那</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许秀云、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">许御乾、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许章清</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、许志永<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">薛爱梅、薛莲霞、薛玉春</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">希尔扎提•巴吾东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">维吾尔族。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年出生于新疆和田。历任新疆维吾尔自治区司法厅长、区党委政法委副书记，新疆维吾尔自治区政协副秘书长。据中国官媒报道，他被指控以中共党员领导干部身份为掩护，长期策划实施分裂国家活动，投靠“东伊运”组织，向境外人员非法提供情报。还将自己受贿所得<span lang="EN-US">120</span>万元和一套房产送给“东伊运”组织使用。并且为服刑人员提供庇护，故意隐瞒服刑人员脱逃的事实，包庇嫌疑人。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日首次披露以“分裂罪”判处希尔扎提•巴吾东死刑缓期二年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">夏霖：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US"> 9</span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 15</span>日出生，贵州省人，北京市华一律师事务所合伙人，维权律师。曾因为人公义正派、代理案件认真有效而在业界有较高知名度；近年来，曾代理过包括艾未未、冉云飞等案在内的多起敏感维权案件；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾为北京市小贩崔英杰杀死城管李志强案做免费辩护律师；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾为刺死官员女服务员邓玉娇涉嫌故意杀人案做代理律师；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾与人权律师浦志强一起为地震义工谭作人辩护；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年人权律师浦志强被中共当局抓捕时，曾为其备选辩护人之一；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，因其为北京传知行社会经济研究所负责人郭玉闪被捕案担任辩护人而被北京市警方突然从家中带走，随后被以涉嫌“赌博”和“诈骗”罪刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日又被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日其案被移送检察院审查起诉，但因证据不足曾被延期三次；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被该法院经一审以“诈骗罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">12</span>万元。其不服上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，经北京第二中级法院二审改判为有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前仍被关押在北京市第一看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">夏忆林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山西太原法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共集团开始迫害法轮功后，两次被判刑，刑期分别为<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月再次被抓捕构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底夏忆林家人收到监狱方电话通知才知已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E6%9B%BE%E4%B8%A4%E6%AC%A1%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E5%A4%AA%E5%8E%9F%E5%A4%8F%E5%BF%86%E6%9E%97%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-434383.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E6%9B%BE%E4%B8%A4%E6%AC%A1%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E5%A4%AA%E5%8E%9F%E5%A4%8F%E5%BF%86%E6%9E%97%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-434383.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">夏月仙</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：武汉市江汉区法轮功学员。年过七旬。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日是中秋节，其带着孙子玩耍，顺便善意地告知民众法轮大法好的真相，遭警察抓捕，被关押到东西湖第一看守所。一年多后，即<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">夏泽红</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：安徽淮南市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，原来是淮南潘二矿职工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日晚发法轮功资料人时，被国保警察抓捕，并把资料和电瓶车推走。在未出示任何证件的情况下，警察非法抄了她的家。后一审被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，上诉，近悉，淮南市中院改为<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">向德斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省咸宁市人，咸宁市咸安区个体出租司机，法轮功学员。因信仰和宣传法轮功备受当局打压迫害，经常被骚扰、跟踪监控。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被咸宁市通城县警方抓捕，之后被送进湖北省法制教育所板桥洗脑班关押，并被进行强行性思想转化迫害。同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被转入咸宁市咸安区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日上午，咸安区法院对向德斌非法庭审，但没有结果。向德斌仍然一直被非法关押在咸安区看守所，至今已经<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">向冬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南省昆明市法轮功学员，女。原是昆明市某房地产公司的高管。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年四十多岁，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年她因发法轮功资料被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。向冬女士这次是因修炼法轮功遭人举报。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被当局抓捕，随后被关押到昆明市看守所。之后西山区国保大队伙同西山区检察院、西山区法院对向冬司法构陷，最后将她判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。这是向冬第二次遭中共邪党法院判刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E4%BA%91%E5%8D%97%E6%98%86%E6%98%8E%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E5%90%91%E5%86%AC%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-445304.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E4%BA%91%E5%8D%97%E6%98%86%E6%98%8E%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E5%90%91%E5%86%AC%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-445304.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">向祚华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，湖北省宜昌市秭归县人，宜昌市秭归县九畹溪镇砚窝台村二组（原芝兰乡芦池湾村三组）村民，冤狱受害人，维权举报人，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年向柞华来因家人与邻居纠纷被宜昌市秭归县警方抓走，并被以涉嫌“故意伤害罪”拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被湖北省宜昌市秭归县法院一审以同罪名判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年；其不服，当庭表示上诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因其向宜昌市中级法院递交了附有新证人名单的刑事上诉状，之后虽经二审，但仍一直不被宣判，直至其在湖北宜昌监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年之后，才将将维持一审判决的二审裁定书交给本人；其不服屡屡申诉，且其辩护律师也将数份足以证明一审判决存在认定事实不清的现场证人证言提交给各级司法部门，但都被耽延未审；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出狱后，因其为讨公道而不惜长期举报、投诉因司法不公被冤狱，然而截至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，最高法院、最高检察院以及宜昌市中级法院均对其申诉驳回请求，以致于其不得不通过网络寻求社会正义力量的关注与支持；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因当局要确保中共“二十大”顺利召开，其遂被秭归县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，至今未放。目前被羁押于湖北省秭归县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/20.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/20.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">项本子：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">工作在广东深圳，原籍湖北省麻城市的法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功，曾经两次在福建省被分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半和<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日下午，在广东省深圳市住宿处，被广东省东莞市长安区乌沙派出所警察，联合广东省国保和东莞市国保，抓捕。项本子被关押在东莞市第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>看守所。据说是因两个月前，项本子在东莞市长安区发放大法法轮功资料，被监控和跟踪。后遭东莞市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，项本子被关押到广东省韶关市北江监狱迫害。之后，家人多次向北江监狱提出会见，监狱方以项本子是法轮功学员，是严管期，不可会见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">项逢选：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1975</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，浙江省台州市仙居县朱溪镇小园村人，网名“皓月”，广州市某洗衣店业主，维权公民，新公民运动参与者。早年因年少气盛，好打抱不平，曾做出过违法行为而被抓捕判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。出狱后前往广东谋生，并在亲友帮助下在广州珠海区开设一家洗衣店。因为人慷慨，极富同情心，经常接济社会底层群众，体会到无钱看病、上学、买房等国计民生问题给普通百姓造成的困惑和巨大压力，遂积极探索社会改革和新公民运动之路。此期间，与张六毛等多位维权人士结成志同道合好友，并经常参与街头围观、抗争声援；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月因在多个<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群中以“皓月”网名积极宣传“要通过武装暴动改变现有体制，走民主宪政之路”，并成立“民选党”，遂遭到广州市当局的疯狂打压；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日与张六毛、苏东亮等多人一同被广州珠海区警方抓捕，张六毛当时被以涉“寻衅滋事”罪由刑拘，而其被涉“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；后被广州市天河区检察院正式批捕，被指控“要以武力推翻现在政权”，“正在制造爆炸物准备搞破坏，对公共安全构成严重的现实危害”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，张六毛被酷刑致死于广州市第三看守所，而其一直没有音信。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日获悉，其已被广州市中级法院以“制造炸弹危害公共安全案主犯”重判。此前被羁押于广州市天河区看守所，目前服刑监狱不详。具体刑期不详，只知刑期很长。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">项锦锋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建维权人士。项锦锋长期帮助和关注弱势群体维权。曾在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被当地国保带走问话，原因涉及他所建的微信群经常谈论政治敏感话题，以及他对公民维权的关注。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，项锦锋在厦门高崎机场海关被限制出境，并被剪掉护照。项锦峰还曾于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日连续<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天被辖区警方传讯，主要调查他在网上发表的“六四”言论，此后项锦峰所在的“风花雪月群”被封杀。项锦锋约于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被拘留在老家龙岩市连城县看守所，涉嫌罪名不详，可能与其网上言论有关。其父母没有收到拘留通知书，只到朋口镇派出所签了字。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_23.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_23.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">肖传雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">福建省宁德市法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底—<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，肖传雄与金丽燕、陈星光、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方从家中抓捕，各人家庭被查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，肖传雄被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。据悉，肖传雄因信法轮功曾已被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并与杨雄一起被关押在福建省龙岩监狱服刑，惨遭狱警残害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，肖传雄被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">肖春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">80</span>后，四川达州公民，长期在福建南安工作生活。热心公义，多年来坚持传播常识，致力推动社会进步，构建公民社会。因<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日在厦门大学门口拉横幅呼吁释放许志永、黄琦、李怀庆、王臧、余文生、程渊、丁家喜、张展等良心犯。并宣传人权、民主、法治等理念，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被福建省南安是警方抓捕。在没有通知家属的情况，被当局以“寻衅滋事”的名义秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，截止目前家属都未曾收到判决书。肖春已于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日移送至福建省漳州监狱服刑。目前其夫人需要照顾家里的<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个孩子和一个老人，成了家里唯一的顶梁柱，一家人生活十分拮据。漳州监狱已疫情为由，停止会见，无奈家属只能写信。但信寄出逾三个月了，没有任何回音，家属非常挂念并担心肖的身体，呼吁当局保障肖春通信等基本权利。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">肖慧君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北唐山市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点钟，唐山丰润区公安局局长刘金良等有计划、有预谋抓捕丰润区法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、付瑞英、尉国申、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺、陆彩芸、韩玉芹、肖慧君等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁的法轮功学员韩玉芹当天被端明路派出所迫害致死。后来，耿福霞、付瑞英、蔚国申以不同的病业形式返回家中；王秀红、陆彩芸、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺被转到唐山第一看守所遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，肖慧君被遵化市法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">肖青山</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：江西省资深的维权人士。在肖青山的维权过程中，近年来多次举横幅要求江西省各级政法机关、及纪检监察机关依法惩治司法中的败类。因为其举横幅喊口号都有出处，也就是<span lang="EN-US">CCTV</span>无时不刻宣扬的那一套，公安国保多次希望他不要举这些横幅，尤其不要上网。从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年“十一”前夕，肖青山就与外界失去了联系，无论朋友们怎样拨打其电话或微信留言，但肖青山的手机与微信始终无应答，朋友们几经周折，终于联系上其家人，证实其已被刑事拘留，目前关押在江西吉安市看守所。但家人不愿意透露更多信息。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其家属获得的逮捕通知书，终于可以确认其是被吉安市公安局青山区分局国保以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”抓捕的事实<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_55.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_55.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_43.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_43.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">肖树清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市北辰区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月因讲法轮功被人举报，曾多次被北辰区瑞景派出所抓捕：有时被劫持去法院；有时去检察院；有时去多个地方检查身体。每次都是经肖树清讲真相当天放回或几天后放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，肖树清又被北辰瑞景派出所抓捕抽血、检查身体；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日再次被瑞景派出所抓捕，没有出示任何字据与凭证，说是“案子”还没结，准备开庭。晚上九点许，瑞景派出所口头通知家属：肖被以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施”判了<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，现被关押在北辰看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">肖艳芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">湖北孝感市汉川市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，肖艳芳、刘义波、王四美、王庆、舒运兰等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人到汉川市马鞍乡联洪村、天成村告诉村民法轮功遭迫害真相及避疫良方，被村民举报，遭马鞍派出所警察抓捕。第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人因疫情原因被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，汉川市公安局对肖艳芳、刘义波、王庆、王四美、舒运兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人下达「监视居住通知书」。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日肖艳芳、刘义波被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，汉川国保人员到湖南长沙，将流落在外打工的法轮功学员王庆抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，汉川市公安局分水派出所警察在分水镇抓捕了王四美和另一名法轮功学员胡汉姣。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，孝昌县法院作出判决，胡汉姣、王四美遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刘义波遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，肖艳芳遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王庆遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。肖艳芳刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">肖艳萍<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西省汉中市法轮功学员，女。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">原是陕西省南郑区大河坎镇长空仪表厂（<span lang="EN-US">76</span>号信箱）职工，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功后，肖艳萍因修炼法轮功，曾先后<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次被中共警察抓捕，多次身陷囹圄，她两次被劳教共<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，两次拘留，加上这次被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，她在中共迫害法轮功的<span lang="EN-US">23</span>年里，竟获刑达<span lang="EN-US">16</span>年半之久。迫害不但使肖艳萍失去公职，且被迫害得家破人亡，她的父亲、丈夫、母亲先后离世。在陕西女子监狱，她遭受各种体罚、精神折磨以及繁重的劳役迫害，受尽屈辱。肖艳萍是在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被汉台公安分局七里派出所警察抓捕的，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前在陕西省女监遭受劳役迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/29/445556.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/29/445556.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">肖永芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省德惠市五台乡法轮功学员。孙桂昌和肖永芬夫妇各被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，已经于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份被羁押到公主岭监狱和吉林省女子监狱。孙桂昌和妻子肖永芬<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被不法警察入室绑架。孙贵昌被送到德惠市拘留所非法拘留五天。肖永芬被送到长春第二看守所检查身体，不合格拒收，第二天下午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多钟放回家，被监视居住。后来，孙桂昌被非法关押德惠看守所。肖永芬因身体和精神状况被放回家，并被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日左右，吉林省公安厅数个警察将在其女儿看家的肖永芬绑架。据悉，肖永芬以前在长春黑嘴子劳教所被迫害得精神失常，现在患有高血压和糖尿病（后期），脚部严重溃烂，现在被关押在吉林省女子监狱八监区；孙桂昌被关押在公主岭监狱九监区。多年来，上述两个监狱公开执法犯法，利用死人床、坐小板凳、长期剥夺睡眠、电棍电击、殴打、上绳等各种酷刑残害和转化善良无辜的法轮功学员，多人被迫害致伤、致残、致疯、致死。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">肖玉霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南昆明市<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，昆明市<span lang="EN-US">5</span>里多派出所及官渡区公安分局国保大队<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个警察闯入肖玉霞家，抢劫大法书籍，并将肖玉霞关进看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>号被官渡分局逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，肖玉霞被<span lang="EN-US">5</span>华法院开庭；判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">肖真义：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年代出生，重庆市人，重庆市两江新区大竹林康美小区公民，重庆市区镇级人大代表独立参选人（之一），重庆绿叶行动志愿者，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，曾因以重庆市合法公民身份积极参选区镇级人大代表换届选举，故引发社会热议，并对其等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位公民的“重庆人大参选独立侯选人联合宣言”给予高度评价和首肯，但终因仅是普通百姓，毫无官场背景或官场背景的支持，而被当地小区以“不合格”为由拒绝报名参选；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因摄录和发布了一段有关当地农贸市场涉及疫情的小视频，而被所住大竹林康美小区派出所警方传唤，并将其手机等当场收走；曾因其未婚女友唐云淑因自家三处房产遭政府强拆损毁而不断维权，遂多次被送进精神病院和被刑拘及判刑，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日其女友又被警方拘捕，在超押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被重庆市丰都县法院以“寻衅滋事罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；此期间，其为营救女友四处奔波呼吁，后因不断为女友喊冤，并持续在网上发声寻求正义和声援，而亦被重庆市两江新区警方抓走失联；后经重庆友人钟声牛与朱春华多方打探，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，终于获知其被重庆市渝北区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕，至今其案已被法院秘密开庭两次，但尚未宣判；据悉，其二位重庆友人钟声牛与朱春华愿为其做代理辩护人，但遭法院拒绝。目前疑似被羁押于重庆市渝北区看守所（重庆市渝北区木耳真木白路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">401127</span>）。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_89.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_89.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢建新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广西桂林市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日半夜，谢建新与妻子赵任远被桂林市七星分局的派出所警察声称“测体温”闯入家中，搜查抄走<span lang="EN-US">1</span>轮功书籍、资料、法轮功币等物品，并抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被庭审，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日均被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢俊彪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川维权人士。因房屋遭强拆从<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年开始上访维权，后关注“六四天网”创办人黄琦冤案，并积极参加营救活动。他因此多次被警方上门警告、传唤、拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，他在微信群中表示自己又被政府警告，说他接受媒体采访，要重点稳控。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日上午，谢俊彪到四川省人大外举牌，牌子上写“戴表（代表）不为民作主 不如回家抓老鼠”。当天下午<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点多，他在成都双流的朋友家里遭社区警察上门抓捕。后谢俊彪遭当地警方刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">30</span>天，后于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，谢俊彪获取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日其取保期马上到期，谢俊彪被双流警方以取保候审期间离开居住地为由，决定刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日家属已被告知其被批准逮捕，当时家属暂未收到逮捕通知书，警察说要寄给谢俊彪的父亲。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东省江门市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，丈夫余荣新被抓捕，关押在江门市看守所，谢清约在<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被抓捕，也被关押在江门市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，在未通知律师和家属的情况下，广东江门法院秘密判刑，余荣新被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年半，妻子谢清被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半。谢清刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">谢清玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，山东泰安市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年六十六岁，泰安市化肥厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午，谢清玲、高方强等法轮功学员去良庄镇赠送法轮功年历，在回来的路上，警察驾驶围堵抓捕。后泰山区公安分局国保大队与岱庙等派出所撬门破锁，闯入谢清玲家中，将家中所有电脑、打印机、法轮功资料等物品抄走。谢清玲和高方强最后被关押到泰安市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉谢清玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款两万元；高方强被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。谢清玲和高方强不服，上诉至泰安市中级法院。泰安中院裁定“维持原判”。后谢清玲转入山东省女子监狱服刑；高方强被转入山东省监狱服刑。谢清玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">谢热扎提<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿海（哈萨克）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年出生，新疆阿尔泰市阿拉哈克乡（<span lang="EN-US">Alagak</span>）人，从事民族特色装修工作者，哈萨克族人权捍卫者、政治犯。因经常频繁与哈萨克斯坦国的亲友联系，遂被当地警方抓捕，并被指控在网上传播暴恐视频等，泄露了国家机密，属于违法行为。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月他被阿尔泰市法院以“泄露国家机密罪”等重判刑期<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。后无任何消息。刑期约至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢文飞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本名谢丰夏。<span lang="EN-US"> 1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，湖南省郴州市桂阳县人，网名“谢文飞”、“南街谢文飞”、“南街谢文飞<span lang="EN-US">@njxwf </span>”，人权捍卫者，南方街头运动践行者，中国政治犯。近年来，因经常活跃于广州街头，勇于为推动中国的民主宪政事业积极发声和献身，故而遭到广东当局的多次打压和拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因前往围观广州公民利瓦伊国申请“六四游行”被拘提起诉讼案开庭，而被广东省佛山市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，关押于佛山市禅诚区看守所，事由是“纪念林昭和曹顺利”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，曾因与民主维权公民王福磊、王默等在广州举牌，发起寻找民主异见人士张圣雨的活动，被石围派出所警方带走，且被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，曾因穿着黑衫在广州市街头拉横幅声援香港民主抗争、“真普选”，被广州警方从增城区新塘镇住所再次带走，并以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；审讯期间，遭酷刑折磨，被广州市越秀看守所警方实施“定镣”处罚，时间长达<span lang="EN-US">104</span>个小时；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，被广州市检察院更换罪名以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式批捕，并被转关至广州市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其案正式开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被广州市中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刑满释放。此前在广东省河源监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日在郴州苏仙区住处突被警方以寻衅滋事罪名刑事拘留，后遭批捕。谢文飞案已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被办案单位苏仙区公安分局移送该院审查起诉，该院已决定以谢文飞“涉嫌寻衅滋事”罪名向苏仙区法院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日本案开庭，开庭时长三小时，未宣判。家属只有谢母能旁听。家属先后聘请谢阳、张磊、任全牛、陈进学律，但均被当局以各种理由排除在外，无法会见、阅卷或出庭。开庭当天由当局指定律师代表谢，但此前谢曾明确拒绝接受官派律师。现羁押在郴州市下辖的资兴市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢阳：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1972</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，湖南省长沙市人，天地人律师事务所和长沙京盈科律师事务所前任律师，原湖南纲维律师事务所律师，人权律师，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年正式执业以来，曾因代理多起公权力滥权案件，如山东省曲阜县薛明凯案、北京新公民运动张宝成案、河南省南乐县南乐教案、湖南省浏阳市张开华征地案等维权案件，并积极关注和参与社会维权运动（包括探访盲人律师陈光诚和声援建三江被捕律师等），而屡遭司法当局阻扰和逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，曾因只身前往山东省东师古村探望盲人律师陈光陈，而被地方黑恶势力殴打抢劫；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾因代理一起民间借贷纠纷案，为维护当事人利益要求取得合议庭商议结果，而被湖南省律师协会罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，并被所在事务所要求解除合同和离职；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾因为“山东薛家命案”作委托代理律师，而被湖南省司法厅当局带走“约谈喝茶”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因为代理湖南省浏阳市土地维权者张开华案，在出庭时遭到当地法院的野蛮阻扰；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因多次代理维权案件，而遭到湖南省律师协会变相打压，不予批准转所手续；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因其积极代理多起长沙市雨花区强制征地拆迁案件，在代理莲湖村农民征地行政诉讼时，曾遭到当地法院非法驱逐；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因其代理广西南宁北部湾建材市场当事人的维权案件，曾遭到多名不明身份人员的持械群殴，致其重伤，右腿骨折，其虽报警，但当地警方却迟迟不予出警；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其在中共“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>大逮捕”中被湖南省长沙市警方抓走，后被以涉嫌“扰乱法庭秩序”、“煽动颠覆国家政权”二罪指定地点监视居住，代理律师要求会见遭拒；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被长沙市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其案在湖南省长沙中级法院开庭受审，但因其被迫当庭认罪，否认曾受酷刑，遂于当日暂获取保候审；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市中级法院正式宣判：犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，但免予刑事处罚；后其虽未被判刑入狱，但仍遭长期软禁和贴身监控；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，曾因去岁年末前往湖南省永顺县声援因发表网络言论而被强制关进精神病院的怀孕女教师李田田，遂被长沙市警方带走失联，其住处遭查抄，许多个人物品均被损毁，两台计算机及一个保险柜被搜走；后其家人收到警方通知，知其已于被抓当日，被长沙市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢阳于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被以“涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕。其</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">代理律师纪中久律师收到长沙市公安局<span lang="EN-US"> 2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日签署的不准予会见的决定书。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，谢阳被控煽动颠覆国家政权罪和寻衅滋事罪被捕。案件目前取保候审被拒、第二次律师会见被拒、扣押的物品归还被拒。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，谢阳辩护人闻宇律师到长沙了解案情，长沙市检察院说，案件还没有到检察院。推测应该是延长了侦查期。然后去看守所，说外地律师一律不让会见。谢阳在看守所的情况，无人知晓。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">目前谢阳被羁押于长沙市第一看守所（湖南省长沙市长沙县泉塘街道远大二路<span lang="EN-US">1736</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">410131</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_41.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_41.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/202246.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/202246.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢志锋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省人，基督徒，安徽省芜湖市基督教某家庭教会事工人员，教会学校老师，中国在押良心犯。因信仰基督，并在安徽省芜湖市基督教一家庭教会的教育学堂事工当老师，随遭中共安徽当局在意识形态方面的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被闯入教学点的芜湖市戈江区警方将包括其在内的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名老师莫名抓走，同时，教学点遭查抄，内中一切物品均被扣押，后其<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人被视为同案嫌疑人统一被芜湖市戈江区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，除杨志言等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名老师被准予取保候审外，谢志锋及王明海等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被芜湖市戈江区检察院以涉嫌“非法经营罪”转正式批捕；据悉，其案已有律师代理。目前被羁押于芜湖市第一看守所（安徽省芜湖市戈江区火龙岗镇白马山村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">241000</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">谢治群：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵州省黔东南苗族侗族自治州（简称黔东南州）凯里市人，基督徒，贵州省凯里市基督复临安息日教会神职人员，教会聚会点传道人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余年前，基督复临安息日教会在贵州省凯里市开始成立聚会点，自此，其一直与教会负责者及多名神职人员通力合作，热忱致力于教会的多种服务工作，尤以带领信徒敬拜和布道为主；但因该教会聚会点长期以来均为家庭教会聚会模式，对中共当局严格把控的“三自教会”管理拒不认同，也不接受（尽管该教会聚会点早已向贵州省宗教局提交请求聚会点合法的申请，但始终莫名未获审批），遂遭贵州当局在意识形态上的严苛限制；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又因该聚会点信徒不断增多，聚会点已由原先的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个剧增到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个，故而很快引起贵州省黔东南州当局的关注与恐慌，并立刻成立项目组，对其聚会点进行全面监控侦查；之后，其及教会长老等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位神职人员均被黔东南州凯里市警方带走，且被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，谢治群等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被凯里市检察院以同罪名予以批捕，控其因所属聚会点申请未被国家审批，众信徒所交善款均属于诈骗款，故其在教会里的一切敬拜布道行为均属违法；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，谢治群<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案在黔东南州凯里市法院统一开庭审理，最终被分别以“诈骗罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">12</span>—<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年不等刑期；其中，谢治群被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月；另其教会<span lang="EN-US">140</span>万余元奉献款亦被宣判扣押；其不服，提起上诉；但据称，黔东南州中级法院似乎不愿对其上诉案公开审理，且对辩护人提交的新证据也无兴趣；二审正在等待中。目前被羁押于黔东南州凯里市看守所（贵州省<span lang="EN-US">/</span>黔东南苗族侗族自治州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>凯里市<span lang="EN-US">/</span>永乐路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">556099</span>）。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杰恩斯汗<span lang="EN-US">. </span>巴格达：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆电视台的哈萨克族配音演员杰恩斯汗<span lang="EN-US">. </span>巴格达因信仰问题也被于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在乌鲁木齐市的家里被公安人员抓走，至今未归，不知下落。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邢果花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张霞、张秀玲、邢果花（现年<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁）三人都是张家口市张北县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下午三点多，张北县国保大队四个警察（便衣），以调查一些事为由，在张霞家楼下强制张霞戴手铐绑架；五点多以同样的手段绑架了法轮功学员邢果花；六点多又绑架了法轮功学员张秀玲。随后讲他们关押到张家口看守所关押；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被到张北县检察院；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被构陷到张北县法院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被张北县法院秘密判刑，张霞<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款三万元；张秀玲<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款两万元，邢果花<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款两万元。张霞向张家口中级法院上诉。邢果花、张秀玲已经于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被转入到石家庄女子监狱迫害。邢果花刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/25/444048.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/25/444048.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邢望力：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，河南省信阳市息县人，又名吴全力，维权访民，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，曾因<span lang="EN-US">7</span>岁幼子邢鉴（时名邢路路）被车祸撞成重伤，地方当局枉法处理且私分赔偿款，自此全家人走上维权道路；因逐级频繁上访，其家数人曾被当局非法拘禁、劳教、判刑等共计达<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年之久，其亦被多次关押拘禁；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因息县维权访民冯国辉在上访期间离奇死于息县农贸市场的出租屋内，邢与妻子等人在网上要求中纪委、公安部等就此事介入彻查，遂惹怒地方当局；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被息县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，指控其尿射县法院名称牌子和抗议法院对其女儿邢梅、母亲及岳母的不公判决等；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事”、“ 敲诈勒索政府”二罪正式逮捕，关押在信阳市息县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其案在河南省信阳市息县法院开审，被一审以“ 敲诈勒索政府罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服立即上，不想次日竟险遭死亡，而狱方事发<span lang="EN-US">10</span>小时后才通知家人，称其在监舍窗口试图用裤子上吊自杀，被人救下时，不慎头朝下重撞头部，致其“右侧额颞叶脑挫裂伤、枕骨骨折、左侧顶部硬膜外血肿、两肺下叶挫伤、双侧胸腔积液，脑组织积水”， 因未脱离危险期家属不得看望；据悉，其在看守所期间，曾屡遭酷刑折磨和牢狱虐待；后经信阳市中级法院二审裁决，“敲诈勒索政府罪”被取消，最终被以“寻衅滋事罪” 判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日刑满释放后，其夫妇因儿子车祸赔偿款遭时任管理者当局贪污，曾数度被投入狱中，遭到当局强力迫害，夫妻二人疾病缠身，无奈之下于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底前往北京寻医治病，但从北京火车站下车便被当地政府截访人员绑架、遣返、拘留，之后又被河南省信阳市息县法院以”困难救济<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>人民币”为定罪依据，以“寻衅滋事罪”将其枉判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；其不服上诉，后经由河南省信阳市中级法院二次密审，依然驳回上诉，维持原判，后送河南省信阳监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，曾因其夫妇二人于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日前往河南省罗山县灵山镇看望被当局软禁<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年有余的人权律师江天勇，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又因在北京市东城区信访投诉，遂再遭北京市前门派出所警员的盘查和拘押，后移交给河南省息县警方，被处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，行政拘留期满日，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转为刑事拘留；后被批捕。目前被羁押于河南省息县看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，邢望力的家属首次见到该判决书：河南省信阳市息县法院认定《致社会各界人士及网友的一封求助信》系虚假信息，诽谤多名公职人员，造成社会恶劣影响，将邢望力以“诽谤罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日；其不服，已提起上诉；二审正在对待中。目前被羁押于河南省息县看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/211.html"><b 11.0pt;">邢文香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">浙江金华圣爱堂牧师包国华的夫人，于<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，邢文香被金华市婺城区法院控告犯有“职务侵占罪”、“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”、“非法经营罪”以及“隐匿会计凭证、会计账簿、财务会计报告罪”等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>项罪名，被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并处没收财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日早上被从家中传唤走的，下午家人前去辖区派出所询问，派出所告知人已经被带走了。何斌、徐彩红夫妻因为租赁纠纷案件一直在北京信访，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被从北京截访人员接回去的，回家后住了一宿再被传唤，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐长禄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁大连市法轮功学员，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1952</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年生，男，家住大连市长海县广鹿乡沙尖村，因修炼法轮功，曾多次遭中共人员抓捕、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日遭抓捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。徐长禄于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬被转入辽南新入监监狱，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">:2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/24/446728.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐德武：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁抚顺市新宾县苇子峪镇法轮功学员。徐德武<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午被当地派出所警察非法带到县公安局，被强行带到抚顺做核酸后，被非法关押在当地看守所，后被抚顺市顺城区检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被抚顺市顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/4/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-423853.html#2142523528-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/4/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-423853.html#2142523528-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">徐福明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">与龚圣亮牧师同案。河南省台前县人，基督教华南教会（<span lang="EN-US">SCC</span>）创建人及钟祥交通会骨干成员。曾因其与多人积极参与基督教华南家庭教会创建和发展活动，在成为湖北省荆门市钟祥市教会骨干之后，又力促教会活动发展至湖北、河南、四川等多个省市，使该教会不仅在人数达<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万信徒，而且在实力上也日趋增强，随引起中共强烈不满和极度恐慌，将华南教会定为“邪教”，其亦在此打击“邪教”行动中遭到严重逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，因被控涉嫌“参与<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月在湖北省钟祥市对受害人谢东报复伤害案”，而被荆门市钟祥市警方以“利用邪教破坏法律实施罪”刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被湖北省荆门市中级法院一审以同罪名判处死刑，<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日又经湖北省荆门市中级法院二审，以“故意伤害罪”改判为无期徒刑，剥夺政治权利终身。目前在湖北省某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐光</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：“八九六四”杭州大学学运领袖，中国民主党浙江委员会核心成员。<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年出生于浙江省富阳市，<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年毕业于杭州大学生物系，大学期间曾参与<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年及<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年学生爱国民主运动，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月在家乡富阳市环保局环境监测站工作的徐光组建了“中国民主党浙江省富阳市筹委会”，是中国民主党第一个县级组织。撰写了《抓不完的中国民主党》等文章，并起草《中国民主党富阳市筹备委员会成立公开宣言》，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被杭州市抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>被逮捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日徐光被以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；出狱后的徐光仍坚守信念，抨击时弊。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日因为在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>上参加中国民主党话题的闲聊，被浙江当局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被正式逮捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日获释，期间从未获准律师会见。后获释。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日徐光遭当地警方于刑事拘留。罪名为涉嫌寻衅滋事。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日徐光被警方正式逮捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日浙江异议人士徐光家属透露，遭羁押的徐光现在绝食已七十多天，转押在杭州市看守所监管医院。此前律师去杭州市西湖区看守所，未能会见到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_87.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; lang="EN-US">31</span>日，遭警方抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，徐桂莲被关押到姚家看守所。此后，大连金州区站前派出所警察和检察院、法院串通，构陷徐桂莲。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月得知，徐桂莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已被劫入位于沈阳于洪区的辽宁省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，南昌市罗家镇徐桂珍等七位法轮功学员在一起学习法轮功著作，被罗家镇派出所警察通过手机定位跟踪，全部被抓捕、抄家。后徐桂珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已被送往江西省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/18/445084.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁大连市法轮功学员，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生，家住大连市普兰店区杨树房街道。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，她遭抓捕，后被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被关押到辽宁女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">:2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/24/446728.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐秦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，原籍湖北武汉，现居江苏扬州市。民间组织“中国人权观察”（筹）前秘书长，“玫瑰团队”成员，人权活动人士，中国在押政治犯。长期以来，一直关注中国人权状况，并与著名人权活动家、民主异议人士秦永敏一道筹建中国人权观察；自秦永敏被捕、秦之妻子赵素利“被失踪”后，她曾多次上街声援，跟进案件；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，当其准备申请旁听隋牧青律师被吊照听证会时，被警方突然限制自由，之后一直遭跟踪与监控；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其在从扬州高邮到昆山的途中被警方带走，后得知其被扬州市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其家属委托的代理律师要求会见，遭到警方拒绝，但被告知其已于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日由刑拘转为“指定居所监视居住”；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又被追加罪名，以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”继续扣留，且不准律师会见；据悉，此次被捕，皆与其近年来坚持关注人权问题，后又积极组织联署声援维权律师余文生，以及为维权公民徐琳筹款等活动有关；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日获悉，其已获取保释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日徐秦被江苏省扬州市中级人民法院指控犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪执行逮捕。现羁押于扬州市看守所。据悉，之前其所涉案件一直处于延审中；又悉，因其刚做完心脏搭桥手术，且患有脑梗、心梗、高血压等多种疾病，故其夫对其身体状况极为担忧。目前被羁押于江苏省扬州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐秦案再次被江苏省扬州市中级法院延长审理期限<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。这是徐秦案第六次被延期，而批准延期的是最高法院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，徐秦的代理律师会见到徐秦。徐秦身体情况不太好，血压不稳，视力、听力都有所下降。徐秦表示自己的所作所为是为了社会进步司法进步，关押期间曾三次绝食抗议。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，纪中久律师在扬州看守所会见了徐秦，得知她于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日瘫痪了。会见时，徐坐在轮椅上，精神疲惫、身体情况很不好。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源： </span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/3.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span
