minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post_34.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post_34.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐瑞萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，广东揭阳法轮功学员。家住揭阳市揭东区曲溪镇路篦村。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，徐瑞萍、被揭东公安分局云路派出所、曲溪派出所警察抓捕，关押到揭东区看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，徐瑞萍被榕城区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，徐瑞萍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，被罚金十万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐润叶：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">宁夏银川市法轮功学员。原籍在内蒙古，系供销社系统退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，徐润叶曾在内蒙古被抓捕，被关押在看守所迫害很长时间。后徐润叶再被抓捕、关押，曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，在宁夏女子监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，徐润叶结束三年半冤狱，从宁夏女子监狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日因张贴法轮功真相传单，被银川市公安局金凤区分局长城中路派出所警察抓捕、构陷，近日被银川市西夏区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前被关押在银川市看守所<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/25/450042.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/25/450042.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐孝兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省高密市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月份，徐孝兰被当地派出所诱骗，说是到所里来一趟，然后被拉到高密市检察院签字，其实签的是批捕的条子。从此，徐孝兰再也没有回家。现在在哪家人和朋友都不知道。经多方打听，徐孝兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，高密市公检法暗箱操作，没有任何消息通知家人，偷偷地判了。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/7/2022-6-7.html#2266222931-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/7/2022-6-7.html#2266222931-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐秀娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">法轮功学员徐秀娟，家在秦皇岛市北港镇，女，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十来岁，因为信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被中共警察抓捕，关押在秦皇岛市第一看守所。被抓捕后，现在在公安医院监护中，徐秀娟的身体处于危险状态，高血压、贫血、心衰，血压最高达到二百四十。亲朋好友一直在找看守所和法院交涉。但是他们互相推诿，拿法轮功学员的生命当儿戏。徐秀娟于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被庭审，遭海港区法院、秦皇岛中级法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被关押到河北石家庄女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">徐永清：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，浙江省龙泉市人，上海市静安区延安西路居民，上海市楼宇建筑弱电专家，上海建瓯信息科技有限公司高级工程师，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。因其个性为人真诚，乐于助人，办事认真且精通业务，故而在任职公司中深受众人好评与尊重，但却因信仰法轮功遭到中共上海当局的严打和监控；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，曾因上海市漕宝路地铁站出现有诬蔑法轮功的画板，出于对自由信仰的维护，其与他人共同向上海市人民大道<span lang="EN-US">200</span>号市政府信访办予以反映，请求撤掉画板，但此举随即遭到上海当局强烈不满和忌恨，并以当时<span lang="EN-US">G20</span>峰会即将召开，“信访时间不合适”为由，将其迅速抓捕并抄家；获释后，因其就<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日中共中央、国务院和公安部联合发布的《公安部关于认定和取缔邪教组织若干问题的通知》（以下简称“取缔”）中罗列的<span lang="EN-US">14</span>种邪教组织名单没有法轮功，也即表明公安部不认为法轮功是邪教，故而针此，其遂于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月向公安部提出“信息公开”申请，并请求公安部对“取缔”一文是否被作废，如若作废，其作废时间和审批程序等予以答复；因公安部一直未给予作答，其遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月以公安部“行政不作为”又向北京市中级法院提出起诉；而此举再次招致中共当局更严厉的打击和报复。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，上海警方以“商谈行政复议”为由将其诱骗至上海市大统路<span lang="EN-US">199</span>号面谈，作完笔录后随即将其以涉嫌“宣传法轮功光盘”为罪由刑拘于海市闸北区看守所；后其虽被释放，但<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其又被扬州市邗江区警方以“从邮局截获<span lang="EN-US">13</span>封法轮功真相信件”为由从家中抓捕刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，被地方检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”正式批捕，并被关押在扬州市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被江苏省扬州市邗江区法院一审以“邪教罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，扬州市中级法院经二审裁决，依然维持原判，后送江苏省洪泽湖监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刑满释放；据悉，其在羁押审讯期间，曾遭酷刑虐待，后在监狱服刑时又被奴役，并遭三次暴力殴打，致身心遭严重受损，会见时几乎站立不住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，当其从老家浙江省龙泉市返回上海的途中，在龙泉火车站被警方再次拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其案被浙江省丽水市莲都区法院开庭审理，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被该法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金一万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月；其不服，已当庭表示上诉；至今二审等待中。目前被羁押于丽水市看守所（浙江省丽水市路湾隧道边，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">323700</span>）。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/4_27.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/4_27.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 349.5pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">徐中惠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省江油市法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年出生，住绵阳江油市武都镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，徐中惠在武都镇出租房内被突然闯入的警察抓捕，并抄家。当时，徐中惠的老母亲就住在徐中惠家，抓捕间，老母亲受惊吓，徐中惠被抓捕走后，老母亲被送到徐中惠的大姐家住，后因惊吓过度去世。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，徐中惠的家属收到徐中惠的辩护律师的电话：江油市法院在<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日判徐中惠<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">4000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">许朝晖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南南阳法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，河南方城县公安局伙抓捕了许朝晖，并抄家。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">许朝晖</span>被关押<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后，转到南阳看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，许朝晖被唐河县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434367.html#2112321541-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434367.html#2112321541-1</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市人，基督徒，哈尔滨市教会音乐学校“麦子圣乐高中”校长，中国在押良心犯；因其所在“麦子圣乐高中”是哈尔滨市一所专门培养基督教音乐人才的艺术学校，尤以教授钢琴最为擅长，学生的培养方向主要是服务教会的唱诗班；然而，自中共新宗教事务条例实施以来，其及其学校频遭所在辖区哈尔滨当局的骚扰和威胁打击；自<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年以来，其家曾被警方两次莫名搜查，且其电话一直被监听；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，麦子圣乐高中突遭辖区内的特警、公安、宗教局、教育局等三四十人的莫名冲击，警方把学校所有老师及学生悉数抓进派出所；其亦在同日早上<span lang="EN-US">7:00</span>左右送孩子上学的路上遭警方拦截抓走，自此失联；后其学校所有学生被讯问后遣回，但其及部分老师被续押，并其极可能会被以“宗教诱骗未成年人”罪名正式刑拘逮捕；之后其学校被查封，所有校财（如钢琴、电脑和资料等）被没收；因至今一直不放，亦毫无音讯，家属急需律师介入；据悉，其在被抓捕前一天，曾提醒老师们警方已经致电房东，让大家做好可能被抓或学校被封的准备，不料次日即被抓捕。目前被羁押地点缺详。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_18.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_18.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许凤梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南周口市东新区法轮功女学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人。家住周口市东新区许湾乡许湾村。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年遭劳教迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被警察入室抓捕、抢劫，关押到周口看守所。接着，邪党公、检、法人员又构陷罪名，将其判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许高瑞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北孝感市孝南区新铺镇政府法轮功学员许章清涂爱莲之子。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚许章清、涂爱莲夫妇、许章清的儿子许高瑞遭警方抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。湖北孝感市下辖安陆市法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下达对许章清<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人的判决：许章清被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，妻子涂爱莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，他们未修炼法轮功的儿子许高瑞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；同时每人还被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。许高瑞刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">许继梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省聊城市冠县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已<span lang="EN-US">73</span>岁。家住聊城市冠县甘官屯镇。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年春天开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份，中共党魁江泽民发动对法轮功修炼者的疯狂迫害。从此周子明、许继梅夫妇遭到甘官屯镇政法委、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”、派出所人员无休止的骚扰：抄家、罚款，威逼他们放弃信仰。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被抓捕，后被冠县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。许继梅的儿女目前也遭迫害，她儿子周春宝之前被抓捕、酷刑折磨得生死不明，女儿周春玲遭抓捕后走脱，现情况不明。多年前，她丈夫也在迫害中离世。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/16/446301.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/16/446301.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许来福：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午案受害人。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2020</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：许来福被判</span>有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">许丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁大连市法轮功女学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，许丽在高新园区摘取中共污蔑法轮功标语，被当地大山村副书记满海柱恶告，高新园区派出所根据监控器查到许丽的车号。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日晚，高新园区派出所<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个警察闯到许丽家，将她抓捕到姚家看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，高新园区法院对许丽判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月在即将结束冤狱时，在没有任何新事件出现的情况下，检察院、法院人员联手无端对许丽判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，使其刑期变成<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，继续将她关押至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/14/446220.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/14/446220.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">许丽华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吉林省榆树市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年七十三岁。二零一一年，许丽华曾被判刑三年，一直在吉林省女子监狱遭迫害三年。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">许丽华在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月疫情期间，在大街上贴法轮功传单，被人诬陷，遭华昌派出所警察抓捕、后“取保候审”。华昌派出所警察仍在继续构陷许丽华老太至德惠市检察院和法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，许丽华老太被德惠市法院判刑三年，已被押入吉林省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-1</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许那（又名许娜）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，当年天安门广场上的绝食学生中，有一位名叫许那（又名许娜），是北京广播学院（现中国传媒大学）的学生。<span lang="EN-US">32</span>年前，她曾和同学高举“新闻自由，言论自由”的横幅，满怀希望地走在北京街头游行的人群中。<span lang="EN-US">32</span>年后，许那仍在北京，却已在东城区看守所被刑事羁押了一年多时间。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，许那和于宙在参加一场同道聚会后双双被拘留四十多天。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，许那因为外地来京的法轮功朋友提供住宿而再次被捕，后被判五年有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年初，随着奥运会的临近，各地异议人士遭到抓捕，包括法轮功修炼者。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚上，于宙、许那在演唱会结束后开车回家的路上，被警方拦住搜查。警察在其车中搜出一本法轮功书籍，将夫妇二人带到通州拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>天后正值除夕，体格健壮的于宙突然离奇死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">42</span>岁。当局声称于宙死于绝食或糖尿病。悲痛欲绝的许那被判处三年有期徒刑。于宙的真实死因至今成谜。于宙、许那的案件见于国际特赦<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月向联合国普遍定期审议递交的报告、美国“国会及行政当局中国委员会”的分析报告、美国国际宗教自由委员会<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年度报告。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，许那第三次被捕。当天<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括许那在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。许那等人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，许那被北京当局宣判，获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/8.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/8.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许秀云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，辽宁抚顺市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，许秀云到李石寨发法轮功真相资料，被警察抓捕，许秀云被关入戒毒所。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，许秀云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，许秀云被关押到辽宁女子监狱，遭受惨无人道的酷刑折磨：<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日下午两点左右，许秀云在西一路交通岗附近给路人免费发送翻墙卡，被两个便衣抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被抚顺市东洲法院开庭，法官田浩以许秀云曾冤狱十三年、出狱未出五年为借口，诬陷其「累犯」，再重判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">许御乾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">广东</span>汕头市澄海区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生。家住汕头市澄海区莲下镇。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共江泽民集团迫害法轮功之后，散布谎言，毒害民众。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，许御乾老人在澄海区莲下镇渡亭村篮球场告诉那里的学生法轮大法好的真相，被受谎言毒害的学生举报，而遭澄海区国保警察抓捕。澄海区国保警察对她家抄家，将她关押在澄海区看守所。今年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，随后被关押在广东省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/3/451439.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/3/451439.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许章清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北孝感市孝南区新铺镇政府公务员，法轮功学员。每天早出晚归，工作兢兢业业几十年。妻子涂爱莲，是孝南区新铺镇远大小学退休教师，退休才<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，在家帮忙带孙女。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚许章清、涂爱莲夫妇、许章清的儿子许高瑞遭警方抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。湖北孝感市下辖安陆市法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下达对许章清<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人的判决：许章清被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，妻子涂爱莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，他们未修炼法轮功的儿子许高瑞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；同时每人还被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。许章清刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许志永：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，河南省商丘市民权县人，前北京邮电学院专业讲师，前北京市海淀区人民法院人民陪审员，“公盟”重要创始人，青年法学家、宪政学者和公民维权代理人，就全国人大对《城市流浪乞讨人员收容遣送办法》进行违宪审查提议者，新公民运动倡导者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其被北京市警方以涉嫌“聚扰乱公共场所秩序罪”刑拘，关押在北京市第三看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被北京市第一中级法院以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，刑满获释；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被广州市警方从番禺海鸥岛杨斌律师处带走；据悉，其此次被抓，疑与<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月曾因参加“厦门聚会案”遭通缉有关，许志永自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日丁家喜律师被捕后就一直在中国南方秘密流亡。其亲友均遭多次骚扰跟踪，其女友李翘楚亦被强迫失踪，后取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被以涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，律师接到临沂市检察院电话：丁、许二案均第二次退回公安补充侦查。许志永现羁押于山东省临沭县看守所。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许志永博士和丁家喜律师因“厦门聚会”被控涉嫌颠覆国家政权案分别于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在山东省临沭县法院进行了不公开开庭审理。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_22.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_22.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">薛爱梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">深圳市南山区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月出生，，会计，家住深圳市南山区桃源街道水木丹华小区。她善良敦厚、学习优异，她原在美国南伊利诺大学读经济学研究生，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，回国探亲时，她派发法轮功真相资料时，遭绑架，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，从此再也没能返回美国完成学业。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，薛爱梅再被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，她被福田区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在广东省女子监狱服刑。她人生最好的年华，都在中共的囚牢中度过。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，薛爱梅乘坐八十一路公交车外出时，发放法轮功资料被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年初，被南山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金五千元。她上诉后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，深圳市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A%E5%9B%B9%E5%9C%84-%E6%B7%B1%E5%9C%B3%E8%96%9B%E7%88%B1%E6%A2%85%E5%86%8D%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-445298.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: minor-fareast;">薛莲霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省青岛市黄岛区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，黄岛区西海岸（原胶南）薛莲霞在大珠山某小区发真相资料时，被一青年人恶意举报。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，薛莲霞被黄岛区大珠山派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午，薛莲霞被取保候审，女儿去派出所交了<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元保证金。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日下午，薛连霞被胁迫去了法院就没回来。她家人听人说，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">薛玉春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省青岛市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生。家住青岛市黄岛区长江路街道办事处张宝湾社区。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共开始发动迫害法轮功，从那时至今，薛玉春至少被中共人员抓捕十次、拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次、骚扰不计其数；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，她被劫持到山东省淄博市王村劳教所劳教两年。她曾遭受残暴酷刑，在<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年前被劳教所折磨致精神失常。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，薛玉春在长江路的多元批发市场给民众讲法轮功真相时，被长江路派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被黄岛区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/3/447182.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/3/447182.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times 11.0pt;">牙里坤<span lang="EN-US">.</span>肉孜（维吾尔）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">闫葵花、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">牙里坤<span lang="EN-US">.</span>肉孜（维吾尔）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆维吾尔自治区人，维吾尔名<span lang="EN-US">Yalqun Rozi</span>，维吾尔族知名作家、讲师和学者，原新疆教育出版社高级编辑，中国在押政治犯。作为高级知识分子，因其长期花费精力编辑了一大批维吾尔人文教科书，发表过若干有关维吾尔文化文章，并于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年帮助编写了中小学校维吾尔教学大纲和语文教学课程，随颇受社会广泛欢迎，并成为维吾尔知识分子中的典范；但自<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月陈全国被任命为新疆党委书记起，因其极左思想将从事维吾尔教科书的工作均视为“意识形态问题的表现”，故而其及众多同行遂遭严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其及其所属教科书编辑公司的全体成员突遭乌鲁木齐市警方抓捕，因抓捕之初并未受到指控，故其涉嫌罪名不详，但自此失联；据悉，因其自被捕至判刑以来，一直无具体信息，故而其身体健康状况及所押地点等均不知情；其家属请求探视、通信权等亦遭拒绝。目前服刑监狱缺详。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，知其被中共新疆当局以“颠覆国家政权罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">闫葵花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省淄博市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，住山东省淄博市临淄区稷下街道闫家村。闫葵花于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被淄博市公安局临淄区分局警察抓捕，关押在淄博市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月中旬，闫葵花被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/22/452228.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/22/452228.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">闫丽君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁锦州凌海法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日生，今年<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁，家住辽宁省凌海市建业乡新安村。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日晚上，建业乡派出所警察和协警，，再次闯入闫丽君家，要把她强行带走。当时，她胳膊摔骨折才两天，还打着石膏。闫丽君被关在锦州市女子看守所，被关押了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，被锦州两级法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被送到辽宁女子新入监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/3/447166.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/3/447166.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">闫琳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江苏盐城市法轮功学员，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1967</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年生，女，退役军人，原盐城市盐都区皮肤病防治所医生。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，法轮功学员闫琳女士被盐城市公安局盐都区分局政保支队抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月下旬，被大丰区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前她仍被关押在大丰区看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/15/447679.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/15/447679.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">闫卫宾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年出生，河南省驻马店市人，原驻马店市政府直属宾馆经理，维权上访者，法轮功学员，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年起，曾因身患乙肝而开始锻炼法轮功，一年后身体复查竟然显示肝功能指标已经正常，故此笃信法轮功；然而，因其追求的宗教信仰与中共政府所宣传的意识形态相左，遂自此屡遭中共公检法部门监控、野蛮抓捕、拘押及劳教等严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因法轮功始遭中共政府迫害，其与家人一同进京请愿和向当局申明法轮功不是邪教，故而被河南警方统一抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，曾因再次进京和平请愿并在天安门打横幅抗议，而被北京警方抓捕，后被以“邪教罪”处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，送北京市团河劳教所（现已更名为北京市监狱团河二监区）关押；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，曾因对他人宣讲法轮功的真相及功用，而被驻马店市驿城区雪松派出所警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因给路人发放法轮功宣传单张，被人举报，遂再被驻马店市驿城区老街派出所警方野蛮抄家、抓走，后被以涉嫌邪教罪名刑拘，并被关押在驻马店市看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其被驻马店市驿城区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，并称其案因是中央“清零行动”直接定下的“政治案”，属河南省“大案要案”，因而必要“重判”；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其案被检察院移交到驻马店市驿城区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案在驿城区法院两次秘审，终被一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年；其不服，上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，经河南省驻马店市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。目前在河南省新乡女子监狱（河南省新乡市化工路与劳动南路交叉口向南一公里，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">453000</span>）服刑。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/7_22.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/7_22.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">闫喜华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省双鸭山市退休女教师，法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬，闫喜华老人在双鸭山集贤县发放法轮功资料时，被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被双鸭山市尖山法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前，闫喜华被关押在双鸭山市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">燕宝萍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：四川攀枝花市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生。原来是攀枝花机电学院校办会计，坚持信仰法轮大法，多次遭绑架、抄家，被开除工作；两次被非法劳教共四年，在四川资中楠木寺女子劳教所遭受到非人折磨。女儿被迫退学。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，燕宝萍在出租房内做法轮功资料时，被攀枝花市东区分局及临江路派出所警察抓捕。之后，燕宝萍被关押到盐边县看守所，后又被转入市看守所，现被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">燕秀红</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河北邢台市广宗县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，广宗县葫芦乡燕红龙村村民。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，广宗县公安局国保带领武警闯入燕秀红的家中，企图抓捕燕秀红。燕秀红在争执中走脱。警察抄走燕秀红的法轮功书籍、现金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元、银行卡<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个、存折<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个和电脑、打印机等物品。燕秀红因此被迫流离失所。到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日燕秀红被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被检察院批捕，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被构陷到法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月燕秀红被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/19/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8C%97%E9%82%A2%E5%8F%B0%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%87%95%E7%A7%80%E7%BA%A2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-431266.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: 0pt;">严英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">宁夏银川市灵武市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US"> 1963</span>年生，是患有严重小儿麻痹后遗症的残疾人。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，严英修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被抓捕、关押构陷；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被吴忠市利通区法院庭审，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。被迫害致乳腺癌、肝囊肿、胆结石，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月入到吴忠市医院。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/24/%E9%81%AD%E7%BB%91%E6%9E%B6%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%A4%E5%B9%B4-%E5%AE%81%E5%A4%8F%E6%AE%8B%E7%96%BE%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%A5%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3%E8%87%B4%E7%99%8C%E7%97%87-433962.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/24/%E9%81%AD%E7%BB%91%E6%9E%B6%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%A4%E5%B9%B4-%E5%AE%81%E5%A4%8F%E6%AE%8B%E7%96%BE%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%A5%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3%E8%87%B4%E7%99%8C%E7%97%87-433962.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">颜会育：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">重庆市渝北区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，颜会育被抓捕到渝北医院体检后，劫持到渝双龙派出所，被关押到渝北区看守所。警察不准她家人接见、不准送钱和衣物。，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月得知她被江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/18/447801.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/18/447801.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">颜志鸿：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1990</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年代出生，广东省人，基督徒，原深圳市某私立学校老师，深圳市某教会信徒，网络活跃人士，社交平台微信公众号运营者，社会良知人士，中国在押良心犯。笃信耶稣基督，并在深圳市某一教会是教会热心信徒；早期曾在深圳市一私立学校当老师，后因活跃于网络平台，而将精力转而投入运营社交平台微信公众号；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，上海疫情“清零”封城期间，因一位旅居上海市的德国人因不满中共当局强制隔离措施引发次生危害，录制了一段英语视频以表抗议，随其看到后将此段英语视频翻译成中文字幕，并上传到自己的微信公众号上，很快引发网络热议，但却使中共当局十分不悦，欲加伺机打击；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其被深圳市国家安全局警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”带走刑拘，至此失联；其他以微信公众号流量谋生的同事及友人亦遭陆续传唤和调查；针此<span lang="EN-US">,</span>其所在深圳某教会发起为期<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天的接力禁食祷告行动<span lang="EN-US">,</span>日期为<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，以期其能早日释放；据悉，其妻因遭胁迫已与警方签署保密协议，不敢对外发声和谈讲任何其在押讯息。目前被羁押地点不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/blog-post_44.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/blog-post_44.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨波：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，广东深圳南山、福田公安警察同时出动，非法抓捕了七位法轮功学员，分别是杨波、肖颖、豆君、朱薏、刘利军（音）、陈小燕与吴治明。其中：刘利军（音）被深圳福田公安抓捕，被关押<span lang="EN-US">39</span>天内获释。吴治明，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，被罗湖公安分局警察绑架并抄家，在罗湖看守所出现高血压，被关押<span lang="EN-US">39</span>天后回家。杨波，善良、热心，从小就乐于助人，也很有正义感。他太太肖颖是某国际知名外企深圳总公司的高管——财务部经理，据说学法轮功时间不长。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>时许，深圳市南山区高新派出所十几个警察（可能包括南山公安分局国保警察）到杨波、肖颖家敲门，警察用冲击钻钻坏两道铁门后，闯入杨波家，在没有出示立案通知书和搜查证的情况下非法抄家。抄走了法轮功书籍、电脑等等私人物品。期间一警察甚至掏出手抢，指向杨波恫吓，也不怕手枪走火。随后，杨波和肖颖夫妻俩被非法抓捕。杨波十三岁的女儿也被警察绑架到派出所几小时，孩子被警察讯问，最后孩子被亲属接回。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，杨波、肖颖、豆君被庭审，四名律师配合默契：三位律师侧重做信仰合法的无罪辩护，辩护很精彩。他们的辩护没被法官打断，但法官似乎心不在焉，没注意听。另一位律师强调办案人员的种种违法行径。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，广东省深圳市中级法院终审判决，维持深圳市南山区法院对上诉人杨波、肖颖定罪量刑的一审判决。杨波被以利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金人民币一万元。其妻子肖颖被以利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并处罚金人民币三千元。杨波刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨成云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。杨成云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年半，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杨大云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，江西九江市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年出生，江西省九江市德安县人，高中文化，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被抓，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年并处罚金一万。杨大云曾经<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年被判刑一年劳教。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.yuanming.net/articles/a160640-%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.yuanming.net/articles/a160640-%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨德新</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：男，江西省宜春市万载县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，江西省万载县罗城镇横坑村人。一九九九年七月二十日中共发动对法轮功的疯狂迫害后，杨德新因坚持对法轮功信仰，遭受了十一年的冤狱迫害：<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，在江西省豫章监狱，杨德新遭受了体罚、辱骂、毒打、悬空吊铐、长时间奴工劳动及强制精神洗脑等各种折磨。杨德新<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被抓捕，后一直被关押在南昌市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初，南昌市第一看守所的在线上账软件显示，杨德新本人已不在看守所，显示「查无此人」。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，杨德新已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，目前可能被非法关押在南昌监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">杨海霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">黑龙江省大庆市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日早晨，杨海霞在家中被捕，关押到杜蒙县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，大庆市让胡路法院判杨海霞刑期<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。杨海霞上诉到大庆市中级法院，九月中旬被枉法裁决：维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，杨海霞被送黑龙江省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/24/2022-2-24.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/24/2022-2-24.html#zip4</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨华明</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：成都法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，在四川省妇幼保健院工作。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，成都市武侯区公安分局晋阳派出所警察和遂宁市射洪县青岗镇派出所警察在杨华明老家抓捕了他。杨华明在被关押期间，武侯区检察院以证据不足两次将材料退回晋阳派出所补充侦察，期间派出所警察和武侯区检察院警察利诱威逼杨华明及其家属：不认罪就重判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，杨华明被武侯区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">:2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨建录：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省张家口市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日下午，杨建录和妻子王惠君在建国街市场讲法轮功，被跟踪他们的宣化县公安分局国保大队警察绑架，家中物品被警察抄走。两天后，王惠君回家，杨建录一直被关押在宣化看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">二零二零年九月四日，杨建录被宣化区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河北省张家口市宣化法院对法轮功学员杨建录判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚金一万元。杨建录家属正在上诉和控告。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/28/446895.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/28/446895.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杨建新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省三门峡市灵宝市人，基督徒，河南灵宝市某基督教归正家庭教会牧师，中国在押良心犯；因其及所在灵宝市某基督教归正家庭教会众信徒不愿接受中共“三自”教会的管控，故而自新宗教事务条例实施以来，即成为屡遭中共当局监控逼迫的家庭教会之一；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年初，因其与当地一家印刷厂联系，以购买一些教会里存放、使用的圣经类书籍，结果不幸被宗教局委派人员监控知道，遂被灵宝市警方以“是印刷书籍的委托责任人”为由从教会中带走刑拘，并被关押于灵宝市看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日<span lang="EN-US">,</span>又被灵宝市检察院以涉嫌“非法经营罪”正式批捕，指控其因为触及印制、购买非法经营之非法出版物，故而其行为已经触犯了国家宗教类法令的相关规定；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其案被灵宝市检察院提起公诉，并将案件移交至河南省三门峡市灵宝市法院审理；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月低<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>月初，被灵宝市法院一审以“非法经营罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服上诉；后经三门峡市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月。目前在河南灵宝市监狱（河南省三门峡市灵宝市，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">472599</span>）服刑。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/56.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/56.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨金德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日出生，河南省南阳市人，南阳市“奥奔”汽车销售有限责任公司（下称奥奔公司）实际控制人、董事长，民营企业家，中国国民党革命委员会（简称“民革党”）成员，南阳市第四届政协委员，前南阳市政法系统廉政监督员，企业维权上访者，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月以来，因创办“奥奔”汽车销售有限责任公司（下称奥奔公司），随着企业绩效日益增高及销售规模不断扩大，其公司随很快成为河南省知名企业，其本人亦成为当地著名的民营企业家，被地方政府看重，并曾被委任为南阳市第四届政协委员和南阳市法院、检察院的廉政监督员；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，曾因一场经济纠纷，其公司集体财产被南阳市卧龙区法院划账私分，且法院院长滥用职权，暴力执法办案，随其公司员工先去银行抗议，继而又去法院投诉，但都毫无果效；其为捍卫员工合法权益，就带领员工连夜进京上访，然而，正是基于此次上访行为，最终导致其及公司众员工遭到的更大厄运；当其被一位南阳市卧龙区副区长带人从北京劝回后，其及公司上下相关员工<span lang="EN-US">22</span>人立即遭遇南阳市警方以“涉黑案”大抓捕；据悉，其被抓之初，曾被旋即送往一警犭基地关押审讯，期间，因长时间惨遭“吊大秤”、“与狼共舞”和“鬼洗脸”等<span lang="EN-US">15</span>种酷刑折磨，导致其身体严重伤残，瘫痪在看守所长达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年之久；其眼耳手脚因多处受伤、断裂、损毁又不给予及时治疗，故而长期无法愈合，直至后来被准予会见新的代理律师时，其左眼视力已坏死，腿脚已萎缩，血压值极高；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月２日<span lang="EN-US">-5</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">23</span>人“涉黑案”在河南省南阳市唐河县法院开庭审理，并被一审以“组织、领导黑社会性质组织罪，聚众扰乱社会秩序罪，妨害作证罪，强迫交易罪，寻衅滋事罪，妨害公务罪”六项罪名分别宣判，其中，其被六罪并罚判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">21</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">40</span>万元；其他<span lang="EN-US">22</span>名被告人分别亦被判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-10</span>年不等刑期或管制或单处罚金；其等<span lang="EN-US">15</span>人不服上诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，知其等多人案经南阳市中级法院二审裁决，虽有所减刑，但其仍被以“组织、领导黑社会性质组织罪，聚众扰乱社会秩序罪，妨害作证罪，强迫交易罪，妨害公务罪”５罪并罚，重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">40</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。目前在河南省第二监狱（河南省新乡市建设路<span lang="EN-US">64</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">453002</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/18.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/18.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨金凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南昌市西湖区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，万筱萍、杨金凤在永正外街，陈丽萍在站前西路锦峰大酒店门口被东湖公安分局抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年元月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，南昌市西湖区法院送达了对陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤及万金莲的刑事判决书，陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，万金莲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。因<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均办理了「取保候审」，刑期均从判决执行之日起算。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杨进香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京延庆法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日生，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，家住北京市延庆区永宁镇。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，杨进香开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚，杨进香和丈夫韩仕民，以及郭金山、吴方玲等被抓捕。郭金山和韩仕民被关押在延庆看守所，杨进香和吴方玲被关押在昌平看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日家人得知，北京延庆区吴方玲、杨进香、韩仕民、郭金山被判刑——吴方玲<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，杨进香<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，韩仕民<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，郭金山<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。杨进香刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/13/447593.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/13/447593.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杨兰英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，云南</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">昆明市法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月出生，云南省曲靖市马龙县人。她曾在昆明煤矿机械总厂马龙分厂经营一家理发店，后因修炼法轮功被非法劳教，理发店被迫关闭。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日在她家中被曲靖市马龙国保、昆明市盘龙国保抄家、抓捕，之后一直被关押在曲靖市麒麟区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，她遭麒麟区法院开庭并判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日送到云南省第二女子监狱继续遭受迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/28/444176.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/28/444176.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨立才：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁籍艺术家、《零八宪章》签署者。杨立才是音像艺术家，曾在北京<span lang="EN-US">798</span>艺术区开设工作室和制品店。杨立才是《零八宪章》签署者，为了追求艺术自由及精神自由，于<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年左右从辽宁漂泊到北京，自创独立音乐场景工作室“白糖罐声场”，成为北京地区活跃的异见艺术家之一。自在法院宣判现场公开声援刘晓波、要求与刘晓波同罪事件后，杨立才受到严密监控。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日北京市第一中级法院宣判刘晓波“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”成立，判处刘晓波有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。刘晓波案宣判后，在法院外声援的杨立才接受采访后向现场的警察投案，要求陪刘晓波坐牢。杨立才后被押往八宝山派出所，做完笔录被限制数小时后于当晚获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初因发表涉港言论遭，杨立才被辽宁省盘锦市警方从深圳抓捕，其在深圳的租住屋遭到查抄，警方查押了他的电脑等物品。后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨立君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">，</b><span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，杨立君与另一名法轮功学员到恒山区柳毛乡安山村、兴开村之间的道路两旁挂真相条幅、树挂、发放真相光盘等资料，被不明真相的人诬告，遭恒山区柳毛派出所抓捕、抄家。后被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。杨立君一直在宣传法轮功，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日又被警察抓捕，家中财物遭劫。至今仍被关押在鸡西市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获悉其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/27/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-441694.html#22426234049-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font:
