minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52182883"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨丽威：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52182883;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省本溪市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，邓玉林、张莉敏、张鹏柱、胡林、杨丽威五位法轮功学员，向当地民众讲清法轮功被迫害真相，去桓仁县散发法轮功资料，被本溪市国保支队、桓仁县国保大队和普乐堡派出所共计抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，邓玉林、胡林被关押在桓仁县看守所，张鹏柱被关押于桓仁县拘留所，杨丽威、张莉敏被关押在本溪市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，胡林被转往沈阳法库县看守所关押。胡林最终被判刑两年。从被抓捕开始，胡林一直在绝食抵制迫害，在被迫害的生命垂危的情况下，被法库县看守所走后门强行送往沈阳康家山监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被沈阳康家山监狱迫害致死。本案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日宣判：邓玉林和杨丽威<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，各罚金二万元，张莉敏<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万五千元，张鹏柱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金一万元。</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨丽威刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨丽霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津法轮功学员。杨丽霞<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日往外挂法轮功挂件时，被南开区长虹派出所警察抓捕。警察又强行抄走家中电脑、打印机、塑封机、大法书籍多本、真相币上千元等其它众多私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日下午五点多钟，杨丽霞被 “取保候审” 放回家，被监视，不准上班。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日接到南开区派出所通知，对她的构陷案件已移交到天津市南开区检察院，在家等消息。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日八点半，杨丽霞在南开区法院被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨丽艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省松原市前郭县白依拉嘎乡红光农场村六分场屯法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被松原市公安局国保大队抓捕，丈夫陈海林（不炼功）也被抓捕，警察抄家，抢劫走<span lang="EN-US">1</span>台笔记本计算机、师父法像、可能还有大法书籍、几部手机等私人物品。杨丽艳被关押在松原市善友看守所。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨明玉：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，山东省聊城地区临清巿人，上访维权人士，零八宪章签署者。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年因发生工伤事故而遇不公，自此加入上访群体，也因此曾被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，被处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">11</span>次。由于在上访过程中屡遭不公与不幸，深感只有追求民主宪政才是唯一的出路，随毅然投入到推进中国民主宪政的事业中，尤其是<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾多次积极参与举牌要求官员财产公示、呼吁公民基本权利等活动。以上行为最终招致当局的不满与忌恨，随于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被深圳市警方秘密拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被深圳巿警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其案在深圳市中级法院开庭审判；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，终被深圳市中级法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。一直被羁押于深圳市福田区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日刑满释放。杨明玉又于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪遭山东临清市警方刑事拘留。被关押在山东临清看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨秋仁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午，广东省广州市天河区法院非法宣判，法轮功学员杨秋仁被判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年有期徒刑。广州市天河区法轮功学员杨秋仁、杨金花，因为通过快递给天河区派出所警察邮寄法轮功学员无辜被迫害的真相资料，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被天河区警方以“破坏法律实施”为由，将两人关押到天河区看守所。杨秋仁今年（<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年）<span lang="EN-US">4</span>岁，江西省丰城市杜市镇人，在广州从事装修方面的工作。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年，杨秋仁在广州第一军医大学炼功点开始修炼法轮功。他做事认真，老实厚道，性格很好。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，中共开始迫害法轮功后，杨秋仁去北京上访，被勒索了<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万多元。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年左右，因为讲述法轮功真相，杨秋仁在广州被绑架，冤判八年，后被劫入江西新建县监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年才结束冤狱回家。本次刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨荣丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，山西省霍州市人，基督徒，前山西师范大学老干部处公职人员，原山西省临汾金灯台家庭教会负责人、传道人，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年全职负责教会以来，将原本几十人的小教会发展成拥有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万名基督徒的大型教会<span lang="EN-US">;2004</span>年，曾因在临汾市兴建金灯台大教堂而遭到当局的严厉打压（含断水断电等各种形式的阻挠）<span lang="EN-US">;2009</span>年，因当局看中该教会所在地商业价值，欲强拆金灯台教堂而被其坚决拒绝，随遭到临汾市浮山县政府的强烈报复，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，竟出动警察<span lang="EN-US">500</span>多名，围堵冲击教会会场和属于该教会的福音鞋厂，殴打致伤百余名基督徒<span lang="EN-US">; </span>后因双方就当地警方野蛮冲击打砸、围殴教会及基督徒的理赔事宜等在协商中发生异议，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日该教会再遭武警包围<span lang="EN-US">; </span>同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因其与<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名教会领袖到太原市上访维权，而被警方在途中劫持<span lang="EN-US">; </span>同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，又被山西省临汾市警方以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">"</span>非法占用农用地罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>、<span lang="EN-US">"</span>聚众扰乱交通秩序罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>刑拘，关押于山西省太原拘留所<span lang="EN-US">; 2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被山西省临汾市尧都区批准以涉嫌同罪名正式批捕<span lang="EN-US">;2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被山西省临汾市尧都区法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，后送往山西省新康监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US">;2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，刑满释放<span lang="EN-US">;2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其与另<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名教会神职人员及负责人、同工等突然又被临汾市尧都区警方莫名带走<span lang="EN-US">; 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。批捕和移送检察院审查起诉的罪名都是涉嫌“诈骗罪”。目前被羁押于山西省临汾市尧都区看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_29.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_29.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杨镕榕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东阳江市法轮功学员，女，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1972</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，是位贤妻良母。她在<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年曾被中共劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，杨镕榕在阳江市江城区牛墟菜市场被南恩派出所人员抓捕、抄家，抢走了一些私人物品，被关押在阳江市白沙看守所。后得知，她已于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底被阳春市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，罚金五千元。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/30/450251.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/30/450251.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨荣霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省石家庄市藁城区法轮功学员。男，家住石家庄市藁城区增村镇杨马村，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，在家中被河北省保定市望都县警察和河北省公安厅警察抓捕。警察抄走两车私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年（具体月份不详），杨荣霞被藁城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现关押于唐山监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">杨雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">福建省宁德市霞浦县人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨贵媚、庄友布、陈开奇，林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，杨雄被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。据悉，此前这<span lang="EN-US">9</span>名法轮功学员之中，杨雄因信法轮功曾被判刑，并与肖传雄一起关押在福建省龙岩监狱服刑，惨遭狱警残害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，杨雄被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨绍政</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日出生，四川省巴中市人，成都市温江区学府尚郡暂住居民，中国农工党党员，西南财经大学经济学博士，前重庆工商大学教师，原贵州大学经济学院教授、硕士生导师和贵州大学高等教育评估与研究专家，贵州大学经济类学科首个被引进人才，中国知名经济学者，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年大学毕业参加工作后，又于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年起进入贵州大学任教，被该校视为经济类学科首个引进的人才以来，一直深得该校的好评和荣耀，然之后因其经常发表令中共当局敏感和忌讳的政治言论，随屡遭贵州当局的监控与维稳打压；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾因网发揭露中共党政人员每年耗费<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万亿元人民币等的相关信息，而被贵州大学叫停授课，且此前就曾因涉政言论而两次被贵州省公安厅约谈和被明确警告在中共<span lang="EN-US">19</span>大期间“闭嘴”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其被贵州大学以发表敏感言论为由正式开除；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年“六四”期间，曾因其在微信群讲<span lang="EN-US">38</span>军军长徐勤先的司机披露说六四杀了<span lang="EN-US">3000-5000</span>名学生，随立刻被贵州省政法委、贵州省网信办及多名警察以“寻衅滋事”为由传唤；传唤中，遭虐待式审讯长达<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个多小时，双手被戴手铐、脚镣，和固定在老虎椅子上，并被要求其衣服脱光、抽血、采集十指指纹及尿检等；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年中共“十·一”期间，曾又遭贵州省政法委控制而软禁多日；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，因杨绍政频发政治敏感言论，虽遭警方警告也不停息，遂再次被贵州省贵阳市花溪区警方秘密带走。自此失联；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，知其被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政府罪”指定居所监视居住。后杨绍政遭正式逮捕。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日杨绍政被贵阳市公安局侦查终结，以涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪移送贵阳市人民检察院审查起诉。辩护律师于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日会见了杨绍政教授。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，贵州省贵阳市人民检察院已经将杨绍政教授涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案件起诉到贵阳市中级法院。杨绍政教授不认为自己有任何违法犯罪行为，杨绍政教授认为如果任由掌握公权的人不受制约的枉法滥权，每一个中国人都有可能受到自己所受到的可怕遭遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">此前杨绍政教授的辩护律师曾代理控告办案人员刑讯逼供、虐待被监管人，贵阳市人民检察院答复称控告不属实。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，辩护律师再次向贵州省人民检察院提起了相关办案人员涉嫌构成刑讯逼供罪、虐待被监管人罪的控告。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，杨绍政涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案在贵阳市中级法院开庭不公开审理，未当庭宣判。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">目前杨绍政被关押在贵阳市乌当区三江农场第一看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_72.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_72.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_42.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_42.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post_76.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post_76.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杨树珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南省昆明市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生，女。朱恩华女士与母亲杨树珍<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在曲靖家中被国保警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，母亲杨树珍被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445958.html%E3%80%81"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445958.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">杨小寒：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">贵州天柱县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年六、七十岁，家住贵州省黔东南州天柱县。在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年下旬，她在贵州省凯里市的一家人家做保姆，带两个小孩，大的五岁，小的三岁。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年临近除夕，杨小寒因教小孩练优美的法轮功功法，被雇主的亲妹妹，一个国保人员，恶告，后被贵州省天柱县公安局抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份左右，在家人不知情的情况下，杨小寒被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/17/2022-2-17.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/17/2022-2-17.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨学华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京西城区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，家住西城区广外。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，杨学华在北京西城区西站附近发送法轮功资料时，被人恶意举报，派出所警察调了一天多摄像头，发现到她。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，杨学华被丰台区太平桥派出所抓捕，二十多个便衣去了她家和她母亲家，非法抄家，抄走许多私人物品。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，杨学华被丰台区法院开庭。在法庭上，律师为杨学华做了无罪辩护，杨学华为自己做了无罪辩护。丰台区法院对杨学华枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。杨学华现仍被关押在丰台区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨玉兴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原在临海市职业技术高中教美术。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年左右，因为校办工厂经营不善面临倒闭，杨玉兴就接手该企业，并迁移到自己位于凌海市（原锦县）南师范街<span lang="EN-US">5</span>栋<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号私有房屋内，办理了工商、税务、环保等手续，用于经营化学试剂分装。另据了解，杨玉兴的该套私有房屋为平房，房产证的建筑面积为<span lang="EN-US">130</span>平米，占地面积<span lang="EN-US">200</span>平米左右。退休教师杨玉兴一直守法经营，照章纳税。到<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，临海市（原锦县）政府官员以城镇化建设为名，与黑社会合起伙来搞房地产开发，他们滥发拆迁许可证，以合法身份掩盖非为目的，通过人民法院在杨玉兴房屋地块违法实施强拆。杨玉兴不服政府官员搞房地产开发的违法乱纪行为，向有关部门举报此事，结果被公安带上手铐游街示众，房屋遭到不法强拆，至今没有任何补偿与安置。<span lang="EN-US"> 2008</span>年奥运会前夕，杨玉兴在北京的出租房子里被临海市的维稳人员跨省抓捕抓回，由公安以“涉嫌寻衅滋事”劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月份，已<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁的杨玉兴老先生，因为在北京邮寄反映地方政府违法拆迁行为，被抓回当地后被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，退休教师的养老金和一切待遇全部被剥夺，当地党政官员还指使黑社会对其女儿进行恐吓。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，已经<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁且失去养老待遇的杨玉兴老先生，从北京回农村老家帮助兄弟地里收粮食，被凌海市公安局刑警队的抓捕，在杨玉兴老先生抓捕后，凌海市公安局也没有给杨玉兴亲属书面通知，临海市检察院作出批捕时，凌海市公安局同样没有把逮捕给予家属书面通知，整个办案过程完全暗箱操作。后由凌海市法院电话告知其女儿，称该院以“寻衅滋事罪”对杨玉兴老先生判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杨运春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省临沂市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，临沂市兰山区庙上村人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，杨运春因发放真相资料被抓捕。后被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，大岭派出所警察给杨运春重新办所谓“取保候审”；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年再次给她办了“取保候审”。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日再次抓捕了杨运春，<span lang="EN-US"> 2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，杨运春被临沂市兰山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/7/450515.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/7/450515.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨智雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">56</span>岁，原是河北《法制日报》社记者，后在石家庄卓达房地产公司主管销售，后在北京某外企公司任办公室主任。因坚持修炼法轮大法，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，妻子祁荭瑾被劳教两年。杨智雄出狱后失去工作，靠打工维持生活，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被骗至保定市所谓“法制教育中心”洗脑班拘禁<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月上旬，他到北京中德环保公司应聘做销售主管，上班不到<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在北京工作单位的宿舍被雄县国保警察郭军学等人抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被雄县法院对杨智开庭。判杨智雄<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月十<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日关押到唐山冀东监狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，杨智雄驾车在容城高速检查站被容城县公安局拘留。在获知其是法轮功学员身份后，上报雄安新区公安局，雄安新区公安局伙同容城公安局、雄县公安局抄了其家。其被抓捕、关押构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，他被劫持到冀东分局第五监狱第五监区。仅一年余，杨智雄被迫害出“骨髓瘤”，身体非常瘦弱。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，家属接到河北省监狱管理局冀东分局第五监狱的电话，说杨智雄病重，住进唐山协和医院重症监护室，让家属去看。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/29/446926.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/29/446926.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">姚爱英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西省南城县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<a name="_Hlk52325061">江西酒厂退休会计。</a><span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始修炼法轮功。姚爱英坚持修炼，曾经多次遭受迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年被<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>六个月。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姚桂珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">上海法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生，家住上海市宝山区。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共邪党开始疯狂迫害法轮功，姚桂珍在上海黄浦公园炼功，被拘留一个月；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年腊月，姚桂珍和十几岁的儿子（儿子还在读中学）遭绑架、抄家，未成年的儿子被关押一个月后，被劫持到上海青浦“洗脑班”迫害。姚桂珍被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，关押在上海女子劳教所，长时间被“关小号”，精神和肉体遭受严重的摧残。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午，姚桂珍遭抓捕，被关押到上海市宝山区看守所。后遭批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，姚桂珍被静安区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姚淑霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江海林市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，海林市老年法轮功学员姚淑霞失联，家人发现家中的大法书籍也不见了。经家人四处打听，一天以后，得知姚淑霞被海林第四派出所抓捕，被拘禁在海林拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被海林市法院开庭，她自辩无罪。仅八天后，法官告诉姚淑霞的家人，姚淑霞已被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，有十天的上诉期。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">姚文田：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1941</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，祖籍不详，现居香港，原香港晨钟书局负责人，中共政治敏感题材出书人，中国在押政治犯。自长期在香港从事出版业以来，因其曾多次出版中共政治敏感题材及部份被中共当局视为禁忌的书籍，如大陆公知作家于建嵘、秦晖、陈志武等撰写的《中国大呼吸——十大学者论国家战略与民族使命》，流亡美国的<span lang="EN-US">89</span>民运人士封从德的《六四日记》，中共前体制内改革派李锐、胡绩伟和谢韬合着的《胡耀邦与中国政治改革——<span lang="EN-US">12</span>位老共产党人的反思》，旅美流亡作家余杰的作品《影帝温家宝》、《河蟹大帝胡锦涛》等等，遂一直被中共当局视为需要打击的异类，其所在出版公司已被赫然列入中共宣传部门需要专项打击的“黑名单”中。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年始，作家余杰的新作《中国教父习近平》封笔，并已商定由香港晨钟书局于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出版发行，此项合作再次触及到中共当局敏感而脆弱的神经，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月诱使他从香港携带七瓶经过改换标签而未经申报的化工品，从罗湖口岸入境，之后在罗湖区与一名张姓人士交接时，被罗湖海关缉私人员当场截获，随后被深圳警方以“携带违禁品” 罪由而拘捕，并被羁押于深圳市某看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，深圳市中级法院开始对其案件予以开庭审理，至<span lang="EN-US">2014 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被以“走私普通货物罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">25</span>万元。目前服刑监狱不明。据悉，其健康状况极差，患有心脏病和哮喘病，并在被拘期间多次晕倒。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">姚忠梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川遂宁市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生，女，姚忠梅与丈夫陈琳于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日早上被安居区国保警察、凤凰派出所等十余人抓捕，并抄家，抢劫走了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>台电脑、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>部手提电脑、两部打印机、几十本大法书籍等私人物品。陈琳、姚忠梅于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被安居区法院秘密开庭，陈琳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，做小生意的轿车（<span lang="EN-US">6</span>～<span lang="EN-US">7</span>万元）、电脑等私人财物被没收；姚忠梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；姚忠梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/23/448001.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/23/448001.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">姚中群：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">重庆市北碚区法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日姚中群被重庆市北碚区国保警察抓捕<span lang="EN-US">,2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被法院开庭判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/24/446659.html#22723233435-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/24/446659.html#22723233435-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">叶尔江•胡阿西：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">新疆伊犁州巩留县人，哈萨克族公民，穆斯林，伊犁州巩留县吉尔格郎乡阿勒玛勒村清真寺伊玛目（即穆斯林集体礼拜时的领祷人或清真寺的教长等领袖人物），中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年起，因中共政府对新疆地区各少数族裔施行更严酷的高压管控政策，遂中共新疆当局开始大规模抓捕维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族穆斯林，清除所有带有少数民族文化特征的标志、广告牌、清真食品，甚至收缴或焚烧《古兰经》，并将数以万计的穆斯林强行送入所谓的“职业技能教育培训中心”（又叫新疆再教育营，休息介绍见面）；接受汉化教育等。对于少数民族聚会，更是设法取缔；后在国际社会关注下，从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年初开始，中共当局被迫将一部分在押培训者予以释放，但于此同时，又将另一部分人予以重判入狱；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其因与所在村落清真寺里的穆斯林共同欢庆每年一度的纳乌鲁斯节（突厥民族的传统节日）时，做了穆斯林特有的敬拜仪式，随后即被伊犁州巩留县吉尔格郎乡警方抓走，同期另有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名清真寺穆斯林亦被抓走，并被悉数送进当地一所“再教育营”接受洗脑培训和关押，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年获悉，其等一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人已被伊犁州巩留县警方以涉嫌“非法集会，传扬不正当的宗教等”罪名予以拘捕，并被伊犁州巩留县检察院起诉至巩留县法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-3</span>月，其等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人案在伊犁州巩留县法院被以“非法集会罪”和“非法传播宗教罪”分别密判<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-21</span>年不等刑期，其中，叶尔江•胡阿西被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">21</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2039</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。目前在新疆新源监狱（新疆伊犁州新源县喀拉布拉镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">835813</span>）服刑。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/21.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/21.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">叶尔灭克﹒木思林：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，新疆昌吉回族自治州木垒县人，回族，木垒县东城镇鸡心梁村村民。因在微信群发出了向往哈萨克斯坦国并希望前往该国等信息，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被木垒县县公安局刑事拘留，自此杳无音讯。据悉，被抓之前，他一无护照，二也从未出境到过哈萨克斯坦国，仅作为一位普通村民，在微信朋友群里发了个帖子，说说个人的想法，并未发表批评政府的言论。其家人说，当地公安以检查为由，先是拿走他的手机，几天后又把他抓走，此后再不知下落，也不准家人见面。截至目前，其一直在押未放。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">叶洪文：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1989</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，广东省汕头市人，本名不详，化名叶隐，推特用户名叶洪文，左派工运支持者，劳工维权声援者，六四纪念受害者，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。因其身为左派工运支持者，在近年来的广东劳工维权与声援活动中，逐渐从对劳工经济的要求转变成对政治的要求，并意识到纪念“六四天安门事件”就是中国劳工运动的“首要部分”，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日发推文称：“六四去中心广场去游行，无论代价。因为这是我的责任，立帖为证”；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，尽管当天户外风雨交加，其依然身着白衣黑裤，手提两个承装祭奠物品的白色塑料袋，额绑红布，来到广东省汕头市人民广场，点燃蜡烛，纪念<span lang="EN-US">8964</span>那些为争取自由民主而牺牲的前辈，并拍下“坦克人”照片发于网上；随后，其即与外界失联；为知其下落，曾有网友多次尝试在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>与微信上与其联系，但都未予回复；原定若被警方带走，其女友就立即代为发推，但也未见发推；后几经辗转终于获知，其因纪念六四，已被汕头市警方带走秘押；迄今为止，其<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>号及相关真实信息已被腾讯公司隐藏，但其推文（尤其是浏览量几十万的示威推文）至今有幸尚存。目前被羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_34.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_34.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">耶尔肯别克•达列力（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">他与玛乌提•么斯尔汗（哈萨克）<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">、</b></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江、哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、肯杰别克﹒达列力都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，</b>肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">伊力哈木•土赫提（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1969</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区阿图什人，原中央民族大学维吾尔族教师，维族学者，维汉双语网站“维吾尔在线”创建人。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年创办维吾尔在线网站，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年新疆乌鲁木齐发生“<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>”事件期间，因该网站被当局视为进行了“大肆煽动宣传，传播谣言”的活动，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，伊力哈木及其家人即被中共当局带走，隔离软禁于北京周边某处，后来在作家王力雄等数百人联署的《关于维吾尔学者伊力哈木•土赫提遭拘押的呼吁》之下，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，才被释放回家；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，又因北京发生天安门撞桥事件，遂于<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在开车带孩子及妻子外出时遭遇国保便衣警察的驾车冲撞及恐吓。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，再次被北京及新疆警察从家中带走刑拘，被羁押于新疆自治区公安厅看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被乌鲁木齐市人民检察院以涉嫌“分裂国家罪”正式批捕，理由是“伊力哈木•土赫提与境外‘东突’势力勾结”，利用互联网鼓吹‘新疆独立’，利用讲堂煽动<span lang="EN-US">'</span>推翻政府<span lang="EN-US">'</span>，利用教师身份从事分裂活动”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，最终被新疆自治区中级法院以“分裂国家罪”重判无期徒刑，没收个人全部财产；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日经二审依然维持原判。目前在新疆自治区第一监狱服刑。其亲属前往探视，送钱及衣服等物品遭狱方拒绝，理由竟是伊力哈木的钱尚未用完，被羁押者无需送衣物。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">伊克帕·阿萨特（维吾尔族）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，新疆维吾尔族自治区乌鲁木齐市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Ekpar Asat</span>，新疆维吾尔族某社群媒体创办人，知名维吾尔族创业家，中国政府眼中的“模范维吾尔公民”， 中国在押政治犯。因被中共官方誉为“模范维吾尔公民”，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，曾多次受邀参加新疆当局举办的各种社会活动，包括曾与新疆政府合办过一场中国与中亚各国之间的拳击比赛等，不仅受到新疆当地民众广泛赞誉，更被中共新疆当局称为能“带来正面影响的人”；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，曾因应邀参加一个由美国国务院举办的有关领导力培训项目，时间为期三周，并在中国代表团中是唯一的少数民族参与者，又因培训期间会见了同在美国哈佛大学完成法学硕士课程的姐姐莱汉·阿萨特（现已是维吾尔族律师，居住在美国首都华盛顿特区），遂在回国三周后，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，突然被失踪，后知被中共新疆乌鲁木齐市警方以涉嫌“极端份子为罪由”刑拘和逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，从中国驻美大使馆回复美国议员库恩斯<span lang="EN-US">(Chris Coons)</span>的电邮中得知，其已被新疆乌鲁木齐市法院以“煽动民族仇恨罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前在新疆自治区乌鲁木齐市某监狱（疑似在新疆第一监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">伊敏江•拉赫米图拉（维吾尔）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区<span lang="EN-US">/</span>克孜勒苏柯尔克孜自治州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>阿图什市人，维吾尔族，新疆福江果业集团有限公司、新疆布格拉农产品开发有限公司、布格拉房地产有限公司、布格拉购物中心和新疆喀什大巴扎（维吾尔族语，即集贸市场）等公司创始人、负责者，维吾尔族亿万富豪之<span lang="EN-US">1</span>，知名慈善企业家，中国在押政治犯。早年，曾就读于新疆金融大学（现更名为新疆财经大学金融学院），毕业后，最初在政府部门供职，数年后开始转而从事商业活动；曾投资<span lang="EN-US"> 5000 </span>万元人民币（合<span lang="EN-US">780</span>万美元）成立了新疆福江果业集团有限公司，后又陆续创立了新疆布格拉农产品开发有限公司、布格拉房地产有限公司、布格拉购物中心（<span lang="EN-US">Bughra Commercial Market</span>）及新疆喀什大巴扎等共计<span lang="EN-US">9</span>大公司，不仅丰富了当地维吾尔小区居民的生活供应，而且为当地维吾尔人创造了显着的就业机会，为阿图什等市的贫困人口提供了大量救助资金；此外，还在将新疆南部的农产品及其他产品引入中亚市场方面发挥了主导作用，故而深受新疆政府的极大赞许和肯定；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其突然被新疆阿图什市警方以涉嫌“支持恐怖分子”罪名刑拘，其女儿及其姐妹努尔古丽•拉赫米图拉<span lang="EN-US"> (Nurgul Rahmitulla) </span>亦被拘留；之后其又被阿图什市检察院以同罪名转正式逮捕，指控其在“为个人财产缴纳天课”（即从事慈善事业）时向被囚的维吾尔族政治犯的家属捐款，此行为触犯了政府相关政策和法律法规；后经两年的调查，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年初，终被新疆阿图什中级法院以“支持恐怖分子”和“为恐怖主义准备”罪重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年；其不服，上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，经克孜勒苏柯尔克孜自治州中级法院<span lang="EN-US">2</span>审裁决：驳回上诉，维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月；据悉，被押初期，曾遭酷刑折磨，并在酷刑胁迫下被迫承认了一些“罪行”，以换取其女被释放，但最终其女仍然被判入狱。目前疑似在阿克苏监狱或沙雅监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/20_20.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/20_20.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">依司马伊利<span lang="EN-US">. </span>斯迪克（维吾尔族）： </span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">维吾尔族农民。<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日生，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被羁押，仅仅<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天后，就被新疆英吉沙县法院以宣扬极端主义罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，判刑如此神速，说明他此前很可能已被关在维吾尔人集中营。依司马伊利<span lang="EN-US">. </span>斯迪克被转送监狱半年后，他被同囚的维吾尔人举报在监狱做礼拜，他很生气就骂维吾尔人不团结，结果他又被新疆建设兵团法院以煽动民族仇恨、破坏监管秩序罪等两个罪名增判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，与前罪合并执行<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日止。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">益西曲珍（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">现年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁，女，退休医生。因<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年在西藏首府拉萨协助救援受枪伤的示威藏人，遭到中共警方拘捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被中共拉萨市中级人民法院以间谍罪判处<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年有期徒刑，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。法院方面在审判会上指出，益西曲珍接受西藏流亡政府安全部指派的任务及资助，向安全部提供危害国家安全及利益等方面的情报、信息，其行为已触犯中华人民共和国刑法第一百一十条的规定，构成间谍罪。藏人行政中央网站指出，正在西藏自治区第一监狱（又名：扎其监狱）中服刑的益西曲珍被捕后遭受警察刑讯逼供，并被关押在卫生条件极差、环境非常恶劣的监狱中，导致营养不良，疾病缠身。曾因身体状况极度恶化，被紧急送医。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">易文君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年出生，四川省成都市人，成都市青羊区牧电巷居民，资深职业画家，成都益州书画院前任常务理事，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。早年曾于<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始锻炼法轮功，至<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，因时任中共最高领导人江泽民疯狂迫害、打压法轮功及其信仰者后，其曾因进京上访而被枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；后因坚持自由信仰，且不畏风险，继续宣传法轮功而屡遭地方当局绑架和拘押，然而即便在此情形下，其仍创作出不少优秀画作，深受众人喜爱与好评；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，中共十九大前夕，其家突遭成都市武侯区红牌楼派出所和成都市青羊区草堂派出所两地警方的连手搜查，并于次日，其夫妇二人（其夫丁中斌，原系某高校及某高中物理教师，亦是法轮功信仰者）均被以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，并关押至成都郫县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因成都市青羊区检察院到郫县看守所“过检”，其夫妇才被以监视居住半年方式准予获释回家；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其夫妇二人再被成都市青羊区草堂派出所警方刑拘，后其家遭查抄，家中新购的两台笔记本电脑、七部手机、多年珍藏价值不菲的自画作品、绘画所用的原材料及锻炼所用的法轮功书籍、个人上万元现金及银行卡等等均被洗劫一空；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其夫因转为监视居住而获释放，而其则被青羊区警方以同罪由转正式逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案被成都市青羊区检察院起诉至青羊区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被成都市青羊区法院一审以“组织和利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。目前在四川省女子监狱（四川省简阳市养马镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">641402</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/8.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">尹峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">济南市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日当天，济南市铁路派出所再次抓捕法轮功学员尹峰，警察同时对最近曾与尹峰有过交往的、居住在朝阳小区的法轮功学员程西江陈连美等法轮功学员抄家、抓捕。程西江被抄走打印机、电脑、大法书籍和一些《九评》、《共产主义的终极目的》等物品和书籍。当日下午，尹峰被逼交<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元保证金后回家。程西江、陈连美被关押在济南铁路看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被秘密审判，判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">尹君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省白山市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生，吉林省白山市抚松县人。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年年底，当时<span lang="EN-US">17</span>岁的尹君开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，正读高三的尹君面临高考，被迫辍学；她曾多次被抓捕、关押，两次被劳教、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被判刑。尹君<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被抓捕，关押在长春市第四看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，她两次被长春市朝阳区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉，尹君被长春市朝阳区法院<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月</span>。她已提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日又被转到吉林省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/28/446906.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/28/446906.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">尹兰华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，吉林辽源市龙山区柏林小镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚间<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点多，辽源市向阳公安分局警察郭凯明等人侵入尹兰华的家中，搜查大法书、法轮功资料、法轮功币。尹兰华也被抓捕到向阳公安分局。那里的警察将她双手反背，用铁铐子铐上<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天，对她刑讯逼供后，最后将尹兰华关押到辽源市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月尹兰华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">尹敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">安徽合肥巢湖市法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">尹敏女士是近两年才学习法轮功的新学员，<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年生，家中还有一个<span lang="EN-US">7</span>岁的孩子。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，尹敏和另外两个法轮功学员被巢湖警察抓捕，约<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年后<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，尹敏被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/16/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436892.html#22115225157-1"><b minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，湖北省大冶市保安镇人，枉判上访者，公益维权者。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2015</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因与王芳、耿彩文等人在武汉市黄鹤楼前身着声援屠夫（吴凎）的文化衫，并拍照上传网媒，随于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被警方从家中带走，拘留于大冶市保安镇派出所，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被转为刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批捕，之后其案被大冶市检察院退补后又移送检察院审查起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日审查起诉期满；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其案在湖北省大冶市法院开庭受审。据悉，关押期间曾一直被拒绝律师会见，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日方获会见，知其遭狱警殴打虐待，导致身心伤害巨大。后被羁押于湖北省大冶市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年初才刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪“刑拘”；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其案被大冶市检察院起诉至地方法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其案被湖北省大冶市法院虽开庭审理，久拖至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日；据悉，其在狱中身体状况极差，已被抢救数次。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，湖北大冶看守所告诉尹家人：尹旭安因高血压偏高导致中风住院。尹旭安与父亲及哥哥视频会见后，家人反映尹现在说话口齿不清，基本生活不能自理，需要依靠其他人帮忙，家人心急如焚。尹旭安<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月底已被转入黄州监狱。目前在监狱医院住院，对比<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月份中风时情况有些好转，说话口齿比原来清晰一些，但是还是没有恢复到原来正常状态，脚也无法像原来那样正常行走，另外高血压在<span lang="EN-US">240</span>左右。现能自理，说话口齿不清，其身体情况令人担忧。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_0.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;">殷宝合：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁朝阳市两法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，殷宝合在恒屹家园粘真相贴时，被本小区内的刘宇恶告，朝阳北塔分局警察将殷宝合抓捕到北塔分局，并对殷宝合抄家。殷宝合被一直关押在朝阳市看守所。后殷宝合被北塔分局构陷到双塔区法院后，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日开庭。被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: minor-fareast;">于波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，李国庆的妻子于波和女儿李蕾在开车出门的路上，突然被天津市宁河县公安局国保支队抓捕。随后，宁河区公安分局伙同芦台镇派出所警察又闯入李国庆的家，不仅强抢打印机、传真机等私人物品，还强行没收了他私人所拥有的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>辆车。随后李国庆、女儿李蕾被关押在芦台派出所；妻子于波被刑拘。李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人后来被关押在宁河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，检察院将构陷他们的案卷递交到宁河区法院刑事庭。近日获悉李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口都被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口，被关押、构陷<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多，近日获悉被判刑：李国庆被枉判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年、妻子于波<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、女儿李蕾<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。于波刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E6%9D%8E%E5%9B%BD%E5%BA%86%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%B6%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%83%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-430403.html"><b style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">青岛市胶州市法轮功学员。原家住黑龙江省齐齐哈尔铁锋区。<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，于柏青因讲真相被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年于柏青离开家乡，来到山东省胶州市居住至今。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日胶州市公安局出动百名警察大肆抓捕当地法轮功学员。她在租房处被胶州市北关派出所抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>，他被青岛市黄岛法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年重刑，并罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<a name="_Hlk101728296"><b href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/8.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">于桂兰</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">：</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁抚顺市望花区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1939</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">82</span>岁。于桂兰老人一九九七年十月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，在抚顺市顺城区葛布新地号，于桂兰告诉人们 “法轮大法好，真善忍好”时，被人举报。于桂兰被前来的警车及举报人绑架。警察将于桂兰老人拉回派出所，晚上十点多，才让老人回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，于桂兰老人去抚顺李石开发区发法轮功资料时，被望花雷锋派出所跟踪，绑架到望花雷锋派出所。四个月后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日早上，望花区雷锋派出所警察到于桂兰家，让于桂兰到望花法院去一趟。于桂兰老人到了法院，法院人员将望花检察院对她的起诉书交给了于桂兰。于桂兰老人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在望花区法院第一法庭开庭。于桂兰老人被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，随即被强行关押在看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于海勇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东海阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，海阳市国保警察共抓捕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名法轮功学员，其中包括于海勇和王雪梅夫妻，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年初，于海勇被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/1/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B5%B7%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%A2%81%E8%80%80%E6%95%8F%E7%AD%89%E5%9B%9B%E4%BD%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-440738.html"><b mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">于桂珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，女。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，于桂珍开始修炼法轮功。于桂珍因坚持修炼法轮大法、修心向善，在中共对法轮功的持续迫害中，曾分别于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年两次被长春市黑嘴子女子教养所关押，共计<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年多，她遭到毒打、电刑、体罚，她的胆被恶人打坏，前胸、后背身体组织损伤。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点多，现居长春市的于桂珍，被绿园区西新派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，于桂珍被关押到长春第四看守所<span lang="EN-US">202</span>监室，主管警察李琳。于桂珍被关押期间，绿园区西新派出所警察阻止律师接见。长春市绿园区、朝阳区公安、检察院、法院暗箱操作，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份，于桂珍被朝阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">于华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: lang="EN-US">15</span>日清晨六点多钟，在农安县政府大楼对面，一群国保公安人员抓捕一家三口——蔡玉英、于娇茹母女，和这家老实巴交的男主人。那天，农安县非法抓捕了二十多名法轮功学员。此次非法抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的，长春市政法委书记马延峰亲赴农安县部署非法抓捕行动，七月十三日，农安县政法委、“<span
