minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于淑芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，辽宁朝阳市凌源市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日之前，朝阳市公安局，政法委，<span lang="EN-US">610</span>秘密开会策划迫害，预谋在<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日之前，要抓一批法轮功学员，向中共百年大庆“献礼”；并成立专项行动小组，电话监控，跟踪监视。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日早晨，朝阳市出动大批警力在同一时间对朝阳市法轮功学员及家属实施抓捕、抄家抢劫。据不完全统计，至少有<span lang="EN-US">27</span>名法轮功学员及家属被抓捕。凌源市公安局及派出所动用了大约<span lang="EN-US">50</span>名警察，抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名凌源市法轮功学员。于淑芬是其中之一，被关押在朝阳市女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被凌源市法院远程视频开庭。后得知：于淑芬被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。后上诉，二审被维持原判。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/4/442063.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/4/442063.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于向家：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大连市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年开始修炼法轮大法，性格内向，善良淳朴。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出差乘高铁，被铁路公安查身份证抓捕，当天晚上，被暴力押回住所。警察抄家，抄走两台计算机、两台打印机、两大箱书。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年元旦前后，于向家被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，目前，于向家仍然被关押在姚家看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">于云峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">网名董狐直笔。生于<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年，是哈尔滨著名民主人士。多年来，他常直言不讳的抨击时政，也热心快肠的帮助民运人士。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，于云峰因言获罪被哈尔滨市当局判处劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，其《劳动教养决定书》写道：于云峰“<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日利用手机分别给哈市及外地市<span lang="EN-US">28</span>个手机用户，发送内容为反党反社会主义的短信，其目的是煽动颠覆国家政权，推翻社会主义制度，给社会稳定造成严重后果，严重扰乱社会治安”，“因其反党、反社会主义，根据《劳动教养试行办法》第十条第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>项的规定，决定对其劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。”<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，于云峰又因为在微信群转发谢阳律师受酷刑的消息，于两会前夕<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>号晚上<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点被抓进拘留所行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日到期还不放人，警方又说他诽谤毛泽东诽谤中国政府要再拘十天。于云峰、李佰华夫妇于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日遭哈尔滨市公安局香坊分局以“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。本次夫妇一起被拘留具体事因未明。后于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获悉于云峰、李佰华夫妇均被以寻衅滋事罪名，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月（二审）被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，李佰华于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份已移送黑龙江女子监狱（集训队）服刑。于云峰目前还关押于哈尔滨香坊区看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/202012285.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/202012285.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余爱明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福清市访民。余爱眀因为在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日到福州大酒店找驻闽的中央巡视组，当场被地方政府的截访维稳人员抓走失联。余爱明的儿子得知信息后，向福州市公安局报了警。今天，余爱明的儿子收到福州市公安局安泰派出所出具的受案回执，告知余爱明已被“人民”政府送到福乐园精神病医院，也就是非法拘禁了。据了解，在福建省福州市，因为认为自己合法权益受到不法侵害，而信访维权被囚禁精神病院迫害的有肢体残疾人雷忠林，具有硕士文凭的叶钟，还有已经被囚禁两年多至今未获自由的何观娇、及晋安区的叶明峰、马尾区的朱晚秀、福清市的陈道财、）刘金云，魏英，陈梅云等，据说实际被非法拘禁于精神病院的访民人数达数十人之多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_81.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_81.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余德贞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏石嘴山市惠农区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍在石嘴山市惠农区水城民生片区讲法轮功，贴真相不干胶，被国保大队和园艺派出所便衣警察跟踪抓捕、抄家，当晚三人被放回家。此后，警察便对每位法轮功学员进行暗中监控和跟踪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅等人被国保警察有预谋的抓捕、抄家。刘翠梅是从银川市的家中被警察抓捕到石嘴山市惠农区，在审讯过程中，多次被殴打。当天，余德贞、陈秀萍、史梅兰、刘翠梅被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅再被抓捕，在石嘴山看守所被关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，余德贞、陈秀萍、史美兰、刘翠梅被石嘴山市大武口区法院判刑。余德贞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被罚金三万元；陈秀萍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金二万五千元；史梅兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，被罚金一万元；刘翠梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余凤连：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川宜宾珙县访民。余凤连是因为父亲余大同在</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1952</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年的土地改革时，划分获得了一块山林，父亲去世后，由余凤连和哥哥继承。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2004</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，余凤连发现自己的山林被相邻的五星村村民余兴伍的继承人侵占，就根据“森林法”规定，向下罗乡政府、珙县政府提起反映，请求调查处理，但政府部门一直没有处理。直到</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年后，珙县政府于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2009</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年作出</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">“关于对下罗乡梧桐村四社余友堂与五星村五社武兴菊林权证争议的决定”，余凤连兄妹不服，向宜宾市政府申请复议，被驳回，上诉至宜宾市中级法院，同样被驳回，最后只能走上所谓“信访不信法”之路。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日上午，余凤连，在位于北京东城区东堂子胡同</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">49-1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">号公安部信访接待室上访，被地方截访</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5-6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">个便衣公安强制拷上手铐，以“通辑犯”为名抓捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">30</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日余凤连的家属收到珙县公安局以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留的通知书。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">余光河</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：重庆市人，重庆市巴南区李家沱居民，法轮功学员。因信仰和宣传法轮功信息，长期遭重庆市巴南区当局骚扰、跟踪、劳教等迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，余光河突然被重庆市九龙坡区国保警察抓走，家被查抄，后得知因宣传法轮功信息被以涉邪教罪刑拘，关押在九龙坡区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日其被重庆市九龙坡区法院开庭受审，并被一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。其不服判决，立即提出上诉，但二审仍然维持原判。目前在重庆市永川监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余慧明</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，英文名：<span lang="EN-US">Winnie,Yu Wai Ming</span>，原英属香港籍、现中华人民共和国（香港）籍人，前香港医管局医疗信息部助理行政主任，前香港医管局内科护士、深切治疗部护士，前香港医管局总部<span lang="EN-US">IT</span>部职员，香港医管局员工阵线主席，泛民主派人士，民主派初选案（又称“<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人初选案”）被告之一、中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于香港中文大学医学院护理系；毕业后，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2014</span>年，曾在香港医管局任职内科护士，后又转到深切治疗部任职；并曾言“不理世事”和时事；但自从<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年香港占领行动（又称“雨伞运动”）以来，尤其是<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日香港政府向抗议市民投下了催泪弹，其开始意识到关心社会时政的必要性；后又因<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年香港《逃犯条例》修订引发了百万人大游行，再次促其对社会议题更多关注，随毅然与其他医护人员筹组工会，并出任工会组织主席；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾因不满医管局管理层无视在改用电子派药系统时出现漏洞而使其同事被迫辞职，以及系统人手不足等问题，而申请调职到总部的<span lang="EN-US">IT</span>部任职，以期了解改良一个电子系统的难度，从而更好地在体制中推动改革；曾因<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年冠状病毒疫情在香港蔓延，进而引发相关医护事宜的争议，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，其随发起医护人员大罢工，并于同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又代表卫生服务界参与立法会民主派初选（官方又称“<span lang="EN-US">35+</span>初选”）；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其与<span lang="EN-US">40</span>余名泛民主派人士统一被香港国安处警方以涉嫌“串谋颠覆国家政权罪”拘捕；被控此前因参选立法会民主派区域选举，故而触犯了香港国安法规定；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其又被香港高等法院批准保释，但至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，因其保释期间在<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>（脸书）上发布帖文，被香港当局认为危害国家安全及违反法院的保释条件，遂再次在香港沙田区被收监逮捕；次日，即被西九龙裁判法院撤销保释，并要求再押侯审。目前疑被羁押于荔枝角收押所。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_45.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_45.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">余江帆：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1989</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，女，河南省南阳市籍人，河南省邓州市夏集乡杨河移民村公民，维权访民，人称“访二代”，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，余江帆因支持南水北调西线工程，随其全家从原籍河南省淅川县香花镇搬迁至河南省邓州市夏集乡移民村；搬迁后，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，因发现移民安置房存有重大质量安全隐患问题，余江帆随其父与多位村民前往省政府投诉，讨说法，不料却被当地警方带回，后被以“上访带头人”之名遭拘押、训诫及殴打，不久含恨去世；为完成父亲遗愿，其自此成了“访二代”，并多次依法逐级投诉表达要求，但毫无果效反遭严打；曾<span lang="EN-US">11</span>次被邓州市警方以 “扰乱公共秩序”罪由行政拘留十数日；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，再次被邓州市警方行政拘留后又转刑事拘留，至<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被河南省邓州市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，之后在郑州女子监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，刑满出狱；之后，其为谋生计而前往北京打工，但因其又积极参与北京地区的公民维权活动（如公民聚餐、声援关注良心犯等活动），故频遭北京警方的逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被邓州市警方以“扰乱单位<span lang="EN-US">/</span>公共场所秩序”为由各处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因其与地方政府就村民房屋修缮问题未达成一致（即拒绝地方当局仅就其个人房屋修缮问题提出解决方案，坚持要求政府先对全村<span lang="EN-US">295</span>户房屋进行质量评估，按照评估结果凭现金发放给各户自行修缮，完毕后再解决自己的房屋问题），遂再遭强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，余江帆在河北活动时，再被赶来的邓州市维稳人员拉走遣返，之后先被邓州市警方处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">18</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转正式刑拘，并被送南阳市看守所羁押；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被邓州市检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其之前的在京上访行为有违国家法律，又是累犯，故建议法院应予从重处罚；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，余江帆案在河南省邓州市法院开庭审理，但庭审中因检察院控其三起上访行为均发生在北京，且其一直常驻北京，故而河南省邓州市法院根本无管辖权，其案长时被迫休庭；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被邓州市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日；然而，当其刑期获释日并未被获释，理由是邓州市法院以其上诉南阳市中级法院裁定案件发回重审为由，拒绝对其（以取保候审）予以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，河南省邓州市法院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。目前羁押于河南省南阳市看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/246.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/246.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">余浚聪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳佳士工人。因要求组建独立工会，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被深圳警方以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，同时被刑事拘留的有<span lang="EN-US">14</span>名工人。关押在深圳龙岗区看守所。关押两年未有信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">余荣新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东省江门市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日余荣新被抓捕，关押在江门市看守所，他的妻子谢清约在<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被抓捕，也被关押在江门市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，在未通知律师和家属的情况下，广东江门法院秘密判刑，余荣新被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年半，妻子谢清被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半。余荣新刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余绍萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人，四川成都市大邑县原北街小学教师、法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日中午，余绍萍被大邑县公安局晋原镇派出所警察抓捕，一行五、六个人，一进校门，就开始摄像，校长在门口接待，并指余绍萍的住房。后被抓捕。余绍萍被关押在郫县看守所。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日在大邑县法院被开庭，余绍萍判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/27/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-441694.html#22426234237-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/27/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E5%9B%9B%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-441694.html#22426234237-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">玉杰（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1987</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区比如县人，前比如县公安局公安警务人员，商人，异议人士，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年被西藏自治区那曲地区比如县公安局录用，<span lang="EN-US"> 7</span>年后终因对其所从事的公安警务工作失望而于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年主动辞职，并在比如县城经商；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月以来，由于比如县比如乡莫阿村、孟庆村和达塘乡等地发生多处藏人示威行动，以抗议当局强行开展“爱国再教育、家家挂红旗”的政治宣讲活动，故而警方以涉嫌‘煽动分裂国家罪’和‘破坏社会稳定罪’，以及自<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日以来在比如县多地发生的示威抗议、县学校学生集体抗议、民众绝食示威等事件中“公开发表非法言论”的罪名为由，于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被警方拘捕；<span lang="EN-US"> 2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被西藏自治区高级法院以“煽动分裂国家罪”和“破坏社会稳定罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前在西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宇美霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，山东省昌乐县法轮功学员。家住昌乐县五图镇，是昌乐县第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>职业中专高级教师。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，宇美霞曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并被罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，宇美霞冤狱期满，回到家中，她的退休工资被社保局停发。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日因她继续宣传法轮大法，遭城关派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日她在青州法院被视频开庭，被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/1/441950.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川成都法轮功学员，女<b>。</b></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">袁华秀于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被恶警抓捕，关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年后家属也没接到开庭通知，后来才知道袁华秀于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被成都高新区法院、检察院黑箱操作，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。袁华秀不服冤判，提出上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">袁王柱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省黄冈市黄梅县法轮功学员。湖北省黄梅县大河镇花园山村人，生于<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年，袁王柱修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，袁王柱在发法轮功资料过程中，被村干诬告，遭大河镇派出所及黄梅县国保抓捕，后在黄冈市的武穴市法院被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，如今被关押在湖北省沙洋农场范家台九监遭受迫害。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/21/%E6%B9%96%E5%8C%97%E9%BB%84%E6%A2%85%E5%8E%BF%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E8%A2%81%E7%8E%8B%E6%9F%B1%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-441531.html"><b &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">袁玉芹：</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52324136;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52186693;"><span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被国保跟踪抓捕。姚新人<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚，在龙口市张家沟看守所「突发」脑溢血，在龙口市人民医院被做开颅手术和气管切开术，龙口公安安插四五个警察在医院进行二十四小时监视。姚新人成植物人状态。龙口公安、国保、看守所至今没给家属任何解释。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，袁玉芹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，付秋荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">袁玉芹刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 159.5pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">袁志强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆北碚区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，在北碚区居民住宅小区几处出现法轮功真相粘贴，当地警察怀疑是由袁志强提供，另一女性法轮功学员粘贴的。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，北碚区国保支队警察，闯进袁志强位于北碚区东阳街道磨心坡村的家中，抄走了大法书籍、真相数据和计算机、打印机等物品。袁志强被关押在北碚区三溪口看守所。后得知，袁志强被江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b
